<p><a class="accordion-trigger ques" id="ques281"><strong>Question 282. What Is A Shared Sql Pool? </strong></a></p>
<p><span class="ans"><strong>Answer :</strong></span><p>The data dictionary cache is stored in an area in SGA called the Shared SQL Pool. This will allow sharing of parsed SQL statements among concurrent users.</p></p>
</li><br><br><li class="quesans mb-20">
<p><a class="accordion-trigger ques" id="ques282"><strong>Question 283. What Is Hot Backup And How It Can Be Taken? </strong></a></p>
<p><span class="ans"><strong>Answer :</strong></span><p>Taking backup of archive log files when database is open. For this the ARCHIVELOG mode should be enabled. The following files need to be backed up. All data files. All Archive log, redo log files. All control files.</p></p>
</li><br><br><li class="quesans mb-20">
<p><a class="accordion-trigger ques" id="ques283"><strong>Question 284. List The Optional Flexible Architecture (ofa) Of Oracle Database? Or How Can We Organize The Tablespaces In Oracle Database To Have Maximum Performance ? </strong></a></p>
<p><span class="ans"><strong>Answer :</strong></span><ul>
<li>SYSTEM - Data dictionary tables.</li>
<li>DATA - Standard operational tables.</li>
<li>DATA2- Static tables used for standard operations</li>
<li>INDEXES - Indexes for Standard operational tables.</li>
<li>INDEXES1 - Indexes of static tables used for standard operations.</li>
<li>TOOLS - Tools table.</li>
<li>TOOLS1 - Indexes for tools table.</li>
<li>RBS - Standard Operations Rollback Segments,</li>
<li>RBS1,RBS2 - Additional/Special Rollback segments.</li>
<li>TEMP - Temporary purpose tablespace</li>
<li>TEMP_USER - Temporary tablespace for users.</li>
<li>USERS - User tablespace.</li>
</ul></p>
</li><br><br><li class="quesans mb-20">
<p><a class="accordion-trigger ques" id="ques284"><strong>Question 285. How To Implement The Multiple Control Files For An Existing Database ?</strong></a></p>
<p><span class="ans"><strong>Answer :</strong></span><p>Shutdown the database Copy one of the existing control file to new location Edit Config ora file by adding new control file. name Restart the database.</p></p>
</li><br><br><li class="quesans mb-20">
<p><a class="accordion-trigger ques" id="ques285"><strong>Question 286. What Is Advantage Of Having Disk Shadowing/ Mirroring ? </strong></a></p>
<p><span class="ans"><strong>Answer :</strong></span><p>Shadow set of disks save as a backup in the event of disk failure. In most Operating System if any disk failure occurs it automatically switchover to place of failed disk. Improved performance because most OS support volume shadowing can direct file I/O request to use the shadow set of files instead of the main set of files. This reduces I/O load on the main set of disks.</p></p>
</li><br><br><li class="quesans mb-20">
<p><a class="accordion-trigger ques" id="ques286"><strong>Question 287. How Will You Force Database To Use Particular Rollback Segment ? </strong></a></p>
<p><span class="ans"><strong>Answer :</strong></span><p>SET TRANSACTION USE ROLLBACK SEGMENT rbs_name.</p></p>
</li><br><br><li class="quesans mb-20">
<p><a class="accordion-trigger ques" id="ques287"><strong>Question 288. Why Query Fails Sometimes ? </strong></a></p>
<p><span class="ans"><strong>Answer :</strong></span><p>Rollback segment dynamically extent to handle larger transactions entry loads. A single transaction may wipeout all available free space in the Rollback Segment Tablespace. This prevents other user using Rollback segments.</p></p>
</li><br><br><li class="quesans mb-20">
<p><a class="accordion-trigger ques" id="ques288"><strong>Question 289. What Is The Use Of Record Length Option In Exp Command ? </strong></a></p>
<p><span class="ans"><strong>Answer :</strong></span><p>Record length in bytes.</p></p>
</li><br><br><li class="quesans mb-20">
<p><a class="accordion-trigger ques" id="ques289"><strong>Question 290. How Will You Monitor Rollback Segment Status ? </strong></a></p>
<p><span class="ans"><strong>Answer :</strong></span><p>Querying the DBA_ROLLBACK_SEGS view</p>
<ul>
<li>IN USE - Rollback Segment is on-line.</li>
<li>AVAILABLE - Rollback Segment available but not on-line.</li>
<li>OFF-LINE - Rollback Segment off-line</li>
<li>INVALID - Rollback Segment Dropped.</li>
<li>NEEDS RECOVERY - Contains data but need recovery or corupted.</li>
<li>PARTLY AVAILABLE - Contains data from an unresolved transaction involving a distributed database.</li>
</ul></p>
</li><br><br><li class="quesans mb-20">
<p><a class="accordion-trigger ques" id="ques290"><strong>Question 291. What Is Meant By Redo Log File Mirroring ? How It Can Be Achieved? </strong></a></p>
<p><span class="ans"><strong>Answer :</strong></span><p>Process of having a copy of redo log files is called mirroring. This can be achieved by creating group of log files together, so that LGWR will automatically writes them to all the members of the current on-line redo log group. If any one group fails then database automatically switch over to next group. It degrades performance.</p></p>
</li><br><br><li class="quesans mb-20">
<p><a class="accordion-trigger ques" id="ques291"><strong>Question 292. Which Parameter In Storage Clause Will Reduce No. Of Rows Per Block? </strong></a></p>
<p><span class="ans"><strong>Answer :</strong></span><p>PCTFREE parameter. Row size also reduces no of rows per block.</p></p>
</li><br><br><li class="quesans mb-20">
<p><a class="accordion-trigger ques" id="ques292"><strong>Question 293. What Is Meant By Recursive Hints ? </strong></a></p>
<p><span class="ans"><strong>Answer :</strong></span><p>Number of times processes repeatedly query the dictionary table is called recursive hints. It is due to the data dictionary cache is too small. By increasing the SHARED_POOL_SIZE parameter we can optimize the size of Data Dictionary Cache.</p></p>
</li><br><br><li class="quesans mb-20">
<p><a class="accordion-trigger ques" id="ques293"><strong>Question 294. What Is The Use Of Parfile Option In Exp Command ? </strong></a></p>
<p><span class="ans"><strong>Answer :</strong></span><p>Name of the parameter file to be passed for export.</p></p>
</li><br><br><li class="quesans mb-20">
<p><a class="accordion-trigger ques" id="ques294"><strong>Question 295. What Is A Logical Backup? </strong></a></p>
<p><span class="ans"><strong>Answer :</strong></span><p>Logical backup involves reading a set of database records and writing them into a file. Export utility is used for taking backup and Import utility is used to recover from backup.</p></p>
</li><br><br><li class="quesans mb-20">
<p><a class="accordion-trigger ques" id="ques295"><strong>Question 296. What Is A Rollback Segment Entry ? </strong></a></p>
<p><span class="ans"><strong>Answer :</strong></span><p>It is the set of before image data blocks that contain rows that are modified by a transaction. Each Rollback Segment entry must be completed within one rollback segment. A single rollback segment can have multiple rollback segment entries.</p></p>
</li><br><br><li class="quesans mb-20">
<p><a class="accordion-trigger ques" id="ques296"><strong>Question 297. What Are The Different Kind Of Export Backups? </strong></a></p>
<p><span class="ans"><strong>Answer :</strong></span><ul>
<li><strong>Full back</strong> - Complete database</li>
<li><strong>Incremental </strong>- Only affected tables from last incremental date/full backup date.</li>
<li><strong>Cumulative backup</strong> - Only affected table from the last cumulative date/full backup date.</li>
</ul></p>
</li><br><br><li class="quesans mb-20">
<p><a class="accordion-trigger ques" id="ques297"><strong>Question 298. How Free Extents Are Managed In Ver 6.0 And Ver 7.0 ? </strong></a></p>
<p><span class="ans"><strong>Answer :</strong></span><ul>
<li>Free extents cannot be merged together in Ver 6.0.</li>
<li>Free extents are periodically coalesces with the neighboring free extent in Ver 7.0.</li>
</ul></p>
</li><br><br><li class="quesans mb-20">
<p><a class="accordion-trigger ques" id="ques298"><strong>Question 299. What Is The Use Of Record Option In Exp Command? </strong></a></p>
<p><span class="ans"><strong>Answer :</strong></span><p>For Incremental exports, the flag indirects whether a record will be stores data dictionary tables recording the export.</p></p>
</li><br><br><li class="quesans mb-20">
<p><a class="accordion-trigger ques" id="ques299"><strong>Question 300. What Is The Use Of Rows Option In Exp Command ?</strong></a></p>
<p><span class="ans"><strong>Answer :</strong></span><p>Flag to indicate whether table rows should be exported. If 'N' only DDL statements for the database objects will be created.</p></p>
</li><br><br><li class="quesans mb-20">
<p><a class="accordion-trigger ques" id="ques300"><strong>Question 301. What Is The Use Of Compress Option In Exp Command ? </strong></a></p>
<p><span class="ans"><strong>Answer :</strong></span><p>Flag to indicate whether export should compress fragmented segments into single extents.</p></p>
</li><br><br><li class="quesans mb-20">
<p><a class="accordion-trigger ques" id="ques301"><strong>Question 302. How Does Space Allocation Table Place Within A Block ? </strong></a></p>
<p><span class="ans"><strong>Answer :</strong></span><ul>
<li>Each block contains entries as follows</li>
<li>Fixed block header</li>
<li>Variable block header</li>
<li>Row Header,row date (multiple rows may exists)</li>
<li>PCTEREE (% of free space for row updation in future)</li>
</ul></p>
</li><br><br><li class="quesans mb-20">
<p><a class="accordion-trigger ques" id="ques302"><strong>Question 303. What Is Dictionary Cache ? </strong></a></p>
<p><span class="ans"><strong>Answer :</strong></span><p>Dictionary cache is information about the databse objects stored in a data dictionary table.</p></p>
</li><br><br><li class="quesans mb-20">
<p><a class="accordion-trigger ques" id="ques303"><strong>Question 304. What Is A Control File ? </strong></a></p>
<p><span class="ans"><strong>Answer :</strong></span><p>Database overall physical architecture is maintained in a file called control file. It will be used to maintain internal consistency and guide recovery operations. Multiple copies of control files are advisable.</p></p>
</li><br><br><li class="quesans mb-20">
<p><a class="accordion-trigger ques" id="ques304"><strong>Question 305. What Is Database Buffers ? </strong></a></p>
<p><span class="ans"><strong>Answer :</strong></span><p>Database buffers are cache in the SGA used to hold the data blocks that are read from the data segments in the database such as tables, indexes and clusters DB_BLOCK_BUFFERS parameter in INIT.ORA decides the size.</p></p>
</li><br><br><li class="quesans mb-20">
<p><a class="accordion-trigger ques" id="ques305"><strong>Question 306. How Will You Create Multiple Rollback Segments In A Database ? </strong></a></p>
<p><span class="ans"><strong>Answer :</strong></span><p>Create a database which implicitly creates a SYSTEM Rollback Segment in a SYSTEM tablespace. Create a Second Rollback Segment name R0 in the SYSTEM tablespace. Make new rollback segment available (After shutdown, modify init.ora file and Start database) Create other tablespaces (RBS) for rollback segments. Deactivate Rollback Segment R0 and activate the newly created rollback segments.</p></p>
</li><br><br><li class="quesans mb-20">
<p><a class="accordion-trigger ques" id="ques306"><strong>Question 307. What Is Cold Backup? What Are The Elements Of It? </strong></a></p>
<p><span class="ans"><strong>Answer :</strong></span><p>Cold backup is taking backup of all physical files after normal shutdown of database. We need to take.</p>
<ul>
<li>All Data files.</li>
<li>All Control files.</li>
<li>All on-line redo log files.</li>
<li>The init.ora file (Optional)</li>
</ul></p>
</li><br><br><li class="quesans mb-20">
<p><a class="accordion-trigger ques" id="ques307"><strong>Question 308. What Is Meant By Redo Log Buffer ? </strong></a></p>
<p><span class="ans"><strong>Answer :</strong></span><p>Changes made to entries are written to the on-line redo log files. So that they can be used in roll forward operations during database recoveries. Before writing them into the redo log files, they will first brought to redo log buffers in SGA and LGWR will write into files frequently. LOG_BUFFER parameter will decide the size.</p></p>
</li><br><br><li class="quesans mb-20">
<p><a class="accordion-trigger ques" id="ques308"><strong>Question 309. How Will You Estimate The Space Required By A Non-clustered Tables? </strong></a></p>
<p><span class="ans"><strong>Answer :</strong></span><ul>
<li>Calculate the total header size</li>
<li>Calculate the available dataspace per data block</li>
<li>Calculate the combined column lengths of the average row</li>
<li>Calculate the total average row size.</li>
<li>Calculate the average number rows that can fit in a block</li>
<li>Calculate the number of blocks and bytes required for the table.</li>
<li>After arriving the calculation, add 10 % additional space to calculate the initial extent size for a working table.</li>
</ul></p>
</li><br><br><li class="quesans mb-20">
<p><a class="accordion-trigger ques" id="ques309"><strong>Question 310. How Will You Monitor The Space Allocation ? </strong></a></p>
<p><span class="ans"><strong>Answer :</strong></span><p>By querying DBA_SEGMENT table/view.</p></p>
</li><br><br><li class="quesans mb-20">
<p><a class="accordion-trigger ques" id="ques310"><strong>Question 311. What Is Meant By Free Extent ? </strong></a></p>
<p><span class="ans"><strong>Answer :</strong></span><p>A free extent is a collection of continuous free blocks in tablespace. When a segment is dropped its extents are reallocated and are marked as free.</p></p>
</li><br><br><li class="quesans mb-20">
<p><a class="accordion-trigger ques" id="ques311"><strong>Question 312. What Is The Use Of Ignore Option In Imp Command ? </strong></a></p>
<p><span class="ans"><strong>Answer :</strong></span><p>A flag to indicate whether the import should ignore errors encounter when issuing CREATE commands.</p></p>

</li><br><br><li class="quesans mb-20">
<p><a class="accordion-trigger ques" id="ques347"><strong>Question 348. When Is Cost Based Optimization Triggered?</strong></a></p>
<p><span class="ans"><strong>Answer :</strong></span><p>It's important to have statistics on all tables for the CBO (Cost Based Optimizer) to work correctly. If one table involved in a statement does not have statistics, Oracle has to revert to rule-based optimization for that statement. So you really want for all tables to have statistics right away; it won't help much to just have the larger tables analyzed.</p>
<p>Generally, the CBO can change the execution plan when you:</p>
<ol>
<li>Change statistics of objects by doing an ANALYZE;</li>
<li>Change some initialization parameters (for example: hash_join_enabled, sort_area_size, db_ file_ multi block_ read_count).</li>
</ol></p>
</li><br><br><li class="quesans mb-20">
<p><a class="accordion-trigger ques" id="ques348"><strong>Question 349. How Can One Optimize %xyz% Queries?</strong></a></p>
<p><span class="ans"><strong>Answer :</strong></span><p>It is possible to improve %XYZ% queries by forcing the optimizer to scan all the entries from the index instead of the table. This can be done by specifying hints. If the index is physically smaller than the table (which is usually the case) it will take less time to scan the entire index than to scan the entire table.</p></p>
</li><br><br><li class="quesans mb-20">
<p><a class="accordion-trigger ques" id="ques349"><strong>Question 350. What Enter Package Procedure Does ? </strong></a></p>
<p><span class="ans"><strong>Answer :</strong></span><p>Enter Validate-data in the current validation unit.</p></p>
</li><br><br><li class="quesans mb-20">
<p><a class="accordion-trigger ques" id="ques350"><strong>Question 351. Where Can One Find I/o Statistics Per Table? </strong></a></p>
<p><span class="ans"><strong>Answer :</strong></span><p>The UTLESTAT report shows I/O per tablespace but one cannot see what tables in the tablespace has the most I/O. The $ORACLE_HOME/rdbms/admin/catio.sql script creates a sample_io procedure and table to gather the required information. After executing the procedure, one can do a simple SELECT * FROM io_per_object; to extract the required information. For more details, look at the header comments in the $ORACLE_ HOME/ rdbms/admin/catio.sql script.</p></p>
</li><br><br><li class="quesans mb-20">
<p><a class="accordion-trigger ques" id="ques351"><strong>Question 352. My Query Was Fine Last Week And Now It Is Slow. Why?</strong></a></p>
<p><span class="ans"><strong>Answer :</strong></span><p>The likely cause of this is because the execution plan has changed. Generate a current explain plan of the offending query and compare it to a previous one that was taken when the query was performing well. Usually the previous plan is not available.</p>
<p>Some factors that can cause a plan to change are: </p>
<ul>
<li>Which tables are currently analyzed? Were they previously analyzed? (ie. Was the query using RBO and now CBO?)</li>
<li>Has OPTIMIZER_MODE been changed in INIT.ORA?</li>
<li>Has the DEGREE of parallelism been defined/changed on any table?</li>
<li>Have the tables been re-analyzed? Were the tables analyzed using estimate or compute? If estimate, what percentage was used?</li>
<li>Have the statistics changed?</li>
<li>Has the INIT.ORA parameter DB_FILE_MULTIBLOCK_READ_COUNT been changed?</li>
<li>Has the INIT.ORA parameter SORT_AREA_SIZE been changed?</li>
<li>Have any other INIT.ORA parameters been changed?</li>
<li>What do you think the plan should be? Run the query with hints to see if this produces the required performance.</li>
</ul></p>
</li><br><br><li class="quesans mb-20">
<p><a class="accordion-trigger ques" id="ques352"><strong>Question 353. When Should One Rebuild An Index? </strong></a></p>
<p><span class="ans"><strong>Answer :</strong></span><p>You can run the 'ANALYZE INDEX VALIDATE STRUCTURE' command on the affected indexes - each invocation of this command creates a single row in the INDEX_STATS view. This row is overwritten by the next ANALYZE INDEX command, so copy the contents of the view into a local table after each ANALYZE. The 'badness' of the index can then be judged by the ratio of 'DEL_LF_ROWS' to 'LF_ROWS'.</p></p>
</li><br><br><li class="quesans mb-20">
<p><a class="accordion-trigger ques" id="ques353"><strong>Question 354. What Are The Unrestricted Procedures Used To Change The Popup Screen Position During Run Time ? </strong></a></p>

<p><a class="accordion-trigger ques" id="ques402"><strong>Question 403. What Is The Most Important Module In Oracle Financials? </strong></a></p>
<p><span class="ans"><strong>Answer :</strong></span><p>The General Ledger (GL) module is the basis for all other Oracle Financial modules. All other modules provide information to it. If you implement Oracle Financials, you should switch your current GL system first.GL is relatively easy to implement. You should go live with it first to give your implementation team a chance to be familiar with Oracle Financials.</p></p>

<p><a class="accordion-trigger ques" id="ques404"><strong>Question 405. What Is The Multiorg And What Is It Used For? </strong></a></p>
<p><span class="ans"><strong>Answer :</strong></span><p>MultiOrg or Multiple Organizations Architecture allows multiple operating units and their relationships to be defined within a single installation of Oracle Applications. This keeps each operating unit's transaction data separate and secure.</p>
<p>Use the following query to determine if MuliOrg is intalled:</p>
<p>select multi_org_flag from fnd_product_groups;</p></p>
</li><br><br><li class="quesans mb-20">
<p><a class="accordion-trigger ques" id="ques405"><strong>Question 406. What Is The Difference Between Fields And Flexfields? </strong></a></p>
<p><span class="ans"><strong>Answer :</strong></span><p>A field is a position on a form that one uses to enter, view, update, or delete information. A field prompt describes each field by telling what kind of information appears in the field, or alternatively, what kind of information should be entered in the field. </p>
<p>A flexfield is an Oracle Applications field made up of segments. Each segment has an assigned name and a set of valid values. Oracle Applications uses flexfields to capture information about your organization. There are two types of flexfields: key flexfields and descriptive flexfields.</p></p>
</li><br><br><li class="quesans mb-20">
<p><a class="accordion-trigger ques" id="ques406"><strong>Question 407. Explain Types Of Block In Forms4.0? </strong></a></p>
<p><span class="ans"><strong>Answer :</strong></span><p><strong>Base table Blocks:</strong><br/>
A base table block is one that is associated with a specific database table or view.<br/>
<strong>Control Blocks:</strong><br/>
A control block is a block that is not associated with a database table.</p></p>
</li><br><br><li class="quesans mb-20">
<p><a class="accordion-trigger ques" id="ques407"><strong>Question 408. What Is An Alert? </strong></a></p>
<p><span class="ans"><strong>Answer :</strong></span><p>An alert is a modal window that displays a message notifies the operator of some application condition.</p></p>
</li><br><br><li class="quesans mb-20">
<p><a class="accordion-trigger ques" id="ques408"><strong>Question 409. What Are The Built-in Routines Is Available In Forms 4.0 To Create And Manipulate A Parameter List? </strong></a></p>

<p><a class="accordion-trigger ques" id="ques409"><strong>Question 410. What Is A Navigable Item? </strong></a></p>
<p><span class="ans"><strong>Answer :</strong></span><p>A navigable item is one that operators can navigate to with the keyboard during default navigation, or that Oracle forms can navigate to by executing a navigational built-in procedure.</p></p>
</li><br><br><li class="quesans mb-20">
<p><a class="accordion-trigger ques" id="ques410"><strong>Question 411. What Is A Library In Forms 4.0? </strong></a></p>
<p><span class="ans"><strong>Answer :</strong></span><p>A library is a collection of Pl/SQL program units, including user named procedures, functions &amp; packages.</p></p>
</li><br><br><li class="quesans mb-20">
<p><a class="accordion-trigger ques" id="ques411"><strong>Question 412. How Image_items Can Be Populate To Field In Forms 4.0? </strong></a></p>
<p><span class="ans"><strong>Answer :</strong></span><p>A fetch from a long raw database column PL/Sql assignment to executing the read_image_file built_in procedure to get an image from the file system.</p></p>
</li><br><br><li class="quesans mb-20">
<p><a class="accordion-trigger ques" id="ques412"><strong>Question 413. What Is The Content View And Stacked View? </strong></a></p>
<p><span class="ans"><strong>Answer :</strong></span><p>A content view is the "Base" view that occupies the entire content pane of the window in which it is displayed. A stacked view differs from a content canvas view in that it is not the base view for the window to which it is assigned.</p></p>
</li><br><br><li class="quesans mb-20">
<p><a class="accordion-trigger ques" id="ques413"><strong>Question 414. What Is A Check Box?</strong></a></p>
<p><span class="ans"><strong>Answer :</strong></span><p>A Check Box is a two state control that indicates whether a certain condition or value is on or off, true or false. The display state of a check box is always either "checked" or "unchecked".</p></p>
</li><br><br><li class="quesans mb-20">
<p><a class="accordion-trigger ques" id="ques414"><strong>Question 415. What Is A Canvas-view? </strong></a></p>
<p><span class="ans"><strong>Answer :</strong></span><p>A canvas-view is the background object on which you layout the interface items (text-items, check boxes, radio groups, and so on.) and boilerplate objects that operators see and interact with as they run your form. At run-time, operators can see only those items that have been assigned to a specific canvas. Each canvas, in term, must be displayed in a specific window.</p></p>
</li><br><br><li class="quesans mb-20">
<p><a class="accordion-trigger ques" id="ques415"><strong>Question 416. Explain The Following File Extension Related To Library? </strong></a></p>
<p><span class="ans"><strong>Answer :</strong></span><p>.pll,.lib,.pld<br/>
The library pll files is a portable design file comparable to an fmb form file<br/>
The library lib file is a plat form specific, generated library file comparable to a fmx form file<br/>
The pld file is Txt format file and can be used for source controlling your library files Parameter.</p></p>
</li><br><br><li class="quesans mb-20">
<p><a class="accordion-trigger ques" id="ques416"><strong>Question 417. Explain The Usage Of Where Current Of Clause In Cursors ? </strong></a></p>
<p><span class="ans"><strong>Answer :</strong></span><p>WHERE CURRENT OF clause in an UPDATE,DELETE statement refers to the latest row fetched from a cursor. Database Triggers.</p></p>
</li><br><br><li class="quesans mb-20">
<p><a class="accordion-trigger ques" id="ques417"><strong>Question 418. Name The Tables Where Characteristics Of Package, Procedure And Functions Are Stored ? </strong></a></p>
<p><span class="ans"><strong>Answer :</strong></span><p>User_objects, User_Source and User_error.</p></p>
</li><br><br><li class="quesans mb-20">
<p><a class="accordion-trigger ques" id="ques418"><strong>Question 419. Explain The Two Type Of Cursors ? </strong></a></p>
<p><span class="ans"><strong>Answer :</strong></span><p>There are two types of cursors, Implicit Cursor and Explicit Cursor. PL/SQL uses Implicit Cursors for queries. User defined cursors are called Explicit Cursors. They can be declared and used.</p></p>
</li><br><br><li class="quesans mb-20">
<p><a class="accordion-trigger ques" id="ques419"><strong>Question 420. What Are Two Parts Of Package ? </strong></a></p>
<p><span class="ans"><strong>Answer :</strong></span><p>The two parts of package are PACKAGE SPECIFICATION &amp; PACKAGE BODY. Package Specification contains declarations that are global to the packages and local to the schema. Package Body contains actual procedures and local declaration of the procedures and cursor declarations.</p></p>
</li><br><br><li class="quesans mb-20">
<p><a class="accordion-trigger ques" id="ques420"><strong>Question 421. What Is A Virtual Private Database? </strong></a></p>
<p><span class="ans"><strong>Answer :</strong></span><p>Oracle 8i introduced the notion of a Virtual Private Database (VPD). A VPD offers Fine-Grained Access Control (FGAC) for secure separation of data. This ensures that users only have access to data that pertains to them. Using this option, one could even store multiple companies' data within the same schema, without them knowing about it. VPD configuration is done via the DBMS_RLS (Row Level Security) package. Select from SYS.V$VPD_POLICY to see existing VPD configuration.</p></p>
</li><br><br><li class="quesans mb-20">
<p><a class="accordion-trigger ques" id="ques421"><strong>Question 422. What Is Raise_application_error ? </strong></a></p>
<p><span class="ans"><strong>Answer :</strong></span><p>Raise_application_error is a procedure of package DBMS_STANDARD which allows to issue an user_defined error messages from stored sub-program or database trigger.</p></p>
</li><br><br><li class="quesans mb-20">
<p><a class="accordion-trigger ques" id="ques422"><strong>Question 423. What Is Oracle Label Security? </strong></a></p>
<p><span class="ans"><strong>Answer :</strong></span><p>Oracle Label Security (formerly called Trusted Oracle MLS RDBMS) uses the VPD (Virtual Private Database) feature of Oracle8i to implement row level security. Access to rows are restricted according to a user's security sensitivity tag or label. Oracle Label Security is configured, controlled and managed from the Policy Manager, an Enterprise Manager-based GUI utility.</p></p>
</li><br><br><li class="quesans mb-20">
<p><a class="accordion-trigger ques" id="ques423"><strong>Question 424. Give The Structure Of The Procedure ? </strong></a></p>
<p><span class="ans"><strong>Answer :</strong></span><pre>
PROCEDURE name (parameter list.....)<br/>is<br/>local variable declarations<br/>BEGIN<br/>Executable statements.<br/>Exception.<br/>exception handlers<br/>end;</pre></p>
</li><br><br><li class="quesans mb-20">
<p><a class="accordion-trigger ques" id="ques424"><strong>Question 425. What Is Oem (oracle Enterprise Manager)? </strong></a></p>
<p><span class="ans"><strong>Answer :</strong></span><p>OEM is a set of systems management tools provided by Oracle Corporation for managing the Oracle environment. It provides tools to monitor the Oracle environment and automate tasks (both one-time and repetitive in nature) to take database administration a step closer to "Lights Out" management.</p></p>
</li><br><br><li class="quesans mb-20">
<p><a class="accordion-trigger ques" id="ques425"><strong>Question 426. What Is Pl/sql ? </strong></a></p>
<p><span class="ans"><strong>Answer :</strong></span><p>PL/SQL is a procedural language that has both interactive SQL and procedural programming language constructs such as iteration, conditional branching.</p></p>
</li><br><br><li class="quesans mb-20">
<p><a class="accordion-trigger ques" id="ques426"><strong>Question 427. What Are The Components Of Oem? </strong></a></p>
<p><span class="ans"><strong>Answer :</strong></span><p>Oracle Enterprise Manager (OEM) has the following components:</p>
<ul>
<li>Management Server (OMS): Middle tier server that handles communication with the intelligent agents. The OEM Console connects to the management server to monitor and configure the Oracle enterprise.</li>
<li>Console: This is a graphical interface from where one can schedule jobs, events, and monitor the database. The console can be opened from a Windows workstation, Unix XTerm (oemapp command) or Web browser session (oem_webstage).</li>
<li>Intelligent Agent (OIA): The OIA runs on the target database and takes care of the execution of jobs and events scheduled through the Console.</li>
</ul></p>
</li><br><br><li class="quesans mb-20">
<p><a class="accordion-trigger ques" id="ques427"><strong>Question 428. What Happens If A Procedure That Updates A Column Of Table X Is Called In A Database Trigger Of The Same Table ? </strong></a></p>
<p><span class="ans"><strong>Answer :</strong></span><p>Mutation of table occurs.</p></p>
</li><br><br><li class="quesans mb-20">
<p><a class="accordion-trigger ques" id="ques428"><strong>Question 429. Is It Possible To Use Transaction Control Statements Such A Rollback Or Commit In Database Trigger?why ? </strong></a></p>
<p><span class="ans"><strong>Answer :</strong></span><p>It is not possible. As triggers are defined for each table, if you use COMMIT of ROLLBACK in a trigger, it affects logical transaction processing.</p></p>
</li><br><br><li class="quesans mb-20">
<p><a class="accordion-trigger ques" id="ques429"><strong>Question 430. What Are The Modes Of Parameters That Can Be Passed To A Procedure ? </strong></a></p>
<p><span class="ans"><strong>Answer :</strong></span><p>IN,OUT,IN-OUT parameters.</p></p>
</li><br><br><li class="quesans mb-20">
<p><a class="accordion-trigger ques" id="ques430"><strong>Question 431. Where The Pre_defined_exceptions Are Stored ? </strong></a></p>
<p><span class="ans"><strong>Answer :</strong></span><p>In the standard package.<br/>
Procedures, Functions &amp; Packages ;</p></p>
</li><br><br><li class="quesans mb-20">
<p><a class="accordion-trigger ques" id="ques431"><strong>Question 432. Give The Structure Of The Function ? </strong></a></p>
<p><span class="ans"><strong>Answer :</strong></span><pre>
FUNCTION name (argument list .....) Return datatype is<br/>local variable declarations<br/>Begin<br/>executable statements<br/>Exception<br/>execution handlers<br/>End;</pre></p>
</li><br><br><li class="quesans mb-20">
<p><a class="accordion-trigger ques" id="ques432"><strong>Question 433. Explain How Procedures And Functions Are Called In A Pl/sql Block ? </strong></a></p>
<p><span class="ans"><strong>Answer :</strong></span><p>Function is called as part of an expression.<br/>
sal := calculate_sal ('a822');<br/>
procedure is called as a PL/SQL statement<br/>
calculate_bonus ('A822');</p></p>
</li><br><br><li class="quesans mb-20">
<p><a class="accordion-trigger ques" id="ques433"><strong>Question 434. What Are Advantages Fo Stored Procedures? </strong></a></p>
<p><span class="ans"><strong>Answer :</strong></span><p>Extensibility,Modularity, Reusability, Maintainability and one time compilation.</p></p>
</li><br><br><li class="quesans mb-20">
<p><a class="accordion-trigger ques" id="ques434"><strong>Question 435. What Is An Exception ? What Are Types Of Exception ? </strong></a></p>
<p><span class="ans"><strong>Answer :</strong></span><p>Exception is the error handling part of PL/SQL block. The types are Predefined and user defined. Some of Predefined exceptions are.</p>
<ul>
<li>CURSOR_ALREADY_OPEN</li>
<li>DUP_VAL_ON_INDEX</li>
<li>NO_DATA_FOUND</li>
<li>TOO_MANY_ROWS</li>
<li>INVALID_CURSOR</li>
<li>INVALID_NUMBER</li>
<li>LOGON_DENIED</li>
<li>NOT_LOGGED_ON</li>
<li>PROGRAM-ERROR</li>
<li>STORAGE_ERROR</li>
<li>TIMEOUT_ON_RESOURCE</li>
<li>VALUE_ERROR</li>
<li>ZERO_DIVIDE</li>
<li>OTHERS.</li>
</ul></p>
</li><br><br><li class="quesans mb-20">
<p><a class="accordion-trigger ques" id="ques435"><strong>Question 436. What Are The Pl/sql Statements Used In Cursor Processing ?</strong></a></p>
<p><span class="ans"><strong>Answer :</strong></span><p>DECLARE CURSOR name, OPEN cursor name, FETCH cursor name INTO or Record types, CLOSE cursor name.</p></p>
</li><br><br><li class="quesans mb-20">
<p><a class="accordion-trigger ques" id="ques436"><strong>Question 437. What Are The Components Of A Pl/sql Block ? </strong></a></p>
<p><span class="ans"><strong>Answer :</strong></span><p><strong>PL/SQL Block Contain </strong></p>
<ul>
<li>Declaration Section,</li>
<li>Executable Section,</li>
<li>Exception Handling Section.</li>
</ul>
<p>i.e</p>
<ul>
<li>DECLARE</li>
<li>BEGIN</li>
<li>END;</li>
</ul></p>
</li><br><br><li class="quesans mb-20">
<p><a class="accordion-trigger ques" id="ques437"><strong>Question 438. What Is A Database Trigger ? Name Some Usages Of Database Trigger ? </strong></a></p>
<p><span class="ans"><strong>Answer :</strong></span><p>Database trigger is stored PL/SQL program unit associated with a specific database table. Usages are Audit data modifications, Log events transparently, Enforce complex business rules Derive column values automatically, Implement complex security authorizations. Maintain replicate tables.</p></p>
</li><br><br><li class="quesans mb-20">
<p><a class="accordion-trigger ques" id="ques438"><strong>Question 439. What Is A Cursor ? Why Cursor Is Required ? </strong></a></p>
<p><span class="ans"><strong>Answer :</strong></span><p>Cursor is a named private SQL area from where information can be accessed. Cursors are required to process rows individually for queries returning multiple rows.</p></p>
</li><br><br><li class="quesans mb-20">
<p><a class="accordion-trigger ques" id="ques439"><strong>Question 440. What Is A Cursor For Loop ? </strong></a></p>
<p><span class="ans"><strong>Answer :</strong></span><p>Cursor for loop implicitly declares %ROWTYPE as loop index, opens a cursor, fetches rows of values from active set into fields in the record and closes when all the records have been processed.<br/>
e.g.. FOR emp_rec IN C1 LOOP<br/>
salary_total := salary_total +emp_rec sal;<br/>
END LOOP;</p></p>
</li><br><br><li class="quesans mb-20">
<p><a class="accordion-trigger ques" id="ques440"><strong>Question 441. What Will Happen After Commit Statement ? </strong></a></p>
<p><span class="ans"><strong>Answer :</strong></span><pre>
Cursor C1 is<br/>Select empno,<br/>ename from emp;<br/>Begin<br/>open C1; loop<br/>Fetch C1 into<br/>eno.ename;<br/>Exit When<br/>C1 %notfound;<br/>commit;<br/>end loop;<br/>end;</pre>
<p>The cursor having query as SELECT .... FOR UPDATE gets closed after COMMIT/ROLLBACK.<br/>
The cursor having query as SELECT.... does not get closed even after COMMIT/ROLLBACK.</p>
<p> </p></p>
</li><br><br><li class="quesans mb-20">
<p><a class="accordion-trigger ques" id="ques441"><strong>Question 442. How Packaged Procedures And Functions Are Called From The Following?<br/>
A. Stored Procedure Or Anonymous Block<br/>
B. An Application Program Such A Prc *c, Pro* Cobol<br/>
C. Sql *plus??
</strong></a></p>
<p><span class="ans"><strong>Answer :</strong></span><p>a. PACKAGE NAME.PROCEDURE NAME (parameters);<br>
variable := PACKAGE NAME.FUNCTION NAME (arguments);<br>
EXEC SQL EXECUTE<br>
b.BEGIN<br/>
PACKAGE NAME.PROCEDURE NAME (parameters)<br/>
variable := PACKAGE NAME.FUNCTION NAME (arguments);<br/>
END;<br/>
END EXEC;<br/>
c. EXECUTE PACKAGE NAME.PROCEDURE if the procedures does not have any out/in-out parameters. A function can not be called.</br></br></br></p></p>
</li><br><br><li class="quesans mb-20">
<p><a class="accordion-trigger ques" id="ques442"><strong>Question 443. What Is A Stored Procedure ? </strong></a></p>
<p><span class="ans"><strong>Answer :</strong></span><p>A stored procedure is a sequence of statements that perform specific function.</p></p>
</li><br><br><li class="quesans mb-20">
<p><a class="accordion-trigger ques" id="ques443"><strong>Question 444. What Is Difference Between A Procedure &amp; Function ? </strong></a></p>
<p><span class="ans"><strong>Answer :</strong></span><p>A FUNCTION is always returns a value using the return statement.</p>
<p>A PROCEDURE may return one or more values through parameters or may not return at all.</p></p>
</li><br><br><li class="quesans mb-20">
<p><a class="accordion-trigger ques" id="ques444"><strong>Question 445. What Is Difference Between A Cursor Declared In A Procedure And Cursor Declared In A Package Specification ? </strong></a></p>
<p><span class="ans"><strong>Answer :</strong></span><p>A cursor declared in a package specification is global and can be accessed by other procedures or procedures in a package.</p>
<p>A cursor declared in a procedure is local to the procedure that can not be accessed by other procedures.</p></p>
</li><br><br><li class="quesans mb-20">
<p><a class="accordion-trigger ques" id="ques445"><strong>Question 446. What Are The Cursor Attributes Used In Pl/sql ? </strong></a></p>
<p><span class="ans"><strong>Answer :</strong></span><ul>
<li><strong>%ISOPEN</strong> - to check whether cursor is open or not.</li>
<li><strong>% ROWCOUNT</strong> - number of rows fetched/updated/deleted.</li>
<li><strong>% FOUND</strong> - to check whether cursor has fetched any row. True if rows are fetched.</li>
<li><strong>% NOT FOUND</strong> - to check whether cursor has fetched any row. True if no rows are featched.</li>
</ul>
<p>These attributes are proceeded with SQL for Implicit Cursors and with Cursor name for Explicit Cursors.</p></p>
</li><br><br><li class="quesans mb-20">
<p><a class="accordion-trigger ques" id="ques446"><strong>Question 447. What Are % Type And % Rowtype ? What Are The Advantages Of Using These Over Datatypes? </strong></a></p>
<p><span class="ans"><strong>Answer :</strong></span><p><strong>% TYPE</strong> provides the data type of a variable or a database column to that variable.<br/>
<strong>% ROWTYPE </strong>provides the record type that represents a entire row of a table or view or columns selected in the cursor.</p>
<p><em><strong>The advantages are :</strong></em></p>
<ul>
<li>Need not know about variable's data type</li>
<li>If the database definition of a column in a table changes, the data type of a variable changes accordingly.</li>
</ul></p>
</li><br><br><li class="quesans mb-20">

<p><a class="accordion-trigger ques" id="ques448"><strong>Question 449. What Are The Advantages Of Having A Package ? </strong></a></p>
<p><span class="ans"><strong>Answer :</strong></span><p>Increased functionality (for example,global package variables can be declared and used by any proecdure in the package) and performance (for example all objects of the package are parsed compiled, and loaded into memory once).</p></p>

<p><a class="accordion-trigger ques" id="ques452"><strong>Question 453. What Is Difference Between Procedures And Functions ? </strong></a></p>

<p><a class="accordion-trigger ques" id="ques456"><strong>Question 457. What Is An Utl_file.what Are Different Procedures And Functions Associated With It? </strong></a></p>
<p><span class="ans"><strong>Answer :</strong></span><p>UTL_FILE is a package that adds the ability to read and write to operating system files. Procedures associated with it are FCLOSE, FCLOSE_ALL and 5 procedures to output data to a file PUT, PUT_LINE, NEW_LINE, PUTF, FFLUSH.PUT, FFLUSH.PUT_LINE,FFLUSH.NEW_LINE. Functions associated with it are FOPEN, ISOPEN.</p></p>

<p><a class="accordion-trigger ques" id="ques457"><strong>Question 458. What Are Oracle Precompilers? </strong></a></p>
<p><span class="ans"><strong>Answer :</strong></span><p>Using ORACLE PRECOMPILERS, SQL statements and PL/SQL blocks can be contained inside 3GL programs written in C,C++,COBOL,PASCAL, FORTRAN,PL/1 AND ADA. The Precompilers are known as Pro*C,Pro*Cobol,... This form of PL/SQL is known as embedded pl/sql,the language in which pl/sql is embedded is known as the host language. The prcompiler translates the embedded SQL and pl/sql statements into calls to the precompiler runtime library. The output must be compiled and linked with this library to creator an executable.</p></p>
</li><br><br><li class="quesans mb-20">
<p><a class="accordion-trigger ques" id="ques458"><strong>Question 459. What Is Difference Between A Formal And An Actual Parameter? </strong></a></p>
<p><span class="ans"><strong>Answer :</strong></span><p>The variables declared in the procedure and which are passed, as arguments are called actual, the parameters in the procedure declaration. Actual parameters contain the values that are passed to a procedure and receive results. Formal parameters are the placeholders for the values of actual parameters.</p></p>
</li><br><br><li class="quesans mb-20">
<p><a class="accordion-trigger ques" id="ques459"><strong>Question 460. What Should Be The Return Type For A Cursor Variable. Can We Use A Scalar Data Type As Return Type?</strong></a></p>
<p><span class="ans"><strong>Answer :</strong></span><p>The return type for a cursor must be a record type.It can be declared explicitly as a user-defined or %ROWTYPE can be used. eg TYPE t_studentsref IS REF CURSOR RETURN students%ROWTYPE.</p></p>

<p><span class="ans"><strong>Answer :</strong></span><p>SUBSTR returns a specified portion of a string eg SUBSTR('BCDEF',4) output BCDE INSTR provides character position in which a pattern is found in a string. eg INSTR('ABC-DC-F','-',2) output 7 (2nd occurence of '-')</p></p>
</li><br><br><li class="quesans mb-20">
<p><a class="accordion-trigger ques" id="ques462"><strong>Question 463. What Is Difference Between Sql And Sql*plus? </strong></a></p>
<p><span class="ans"><strong>Answer :</strong></span><p>SQL*PLUS is a command line tool where as SQL and PL/SQL language interface and reporting tool. Its a command line tool that allows user to type SQL commands to be executed directly against an Oracle database. SQL is a language used to query the relational database(DML,DCL,DDL). SQL*PLUS commands are used to format query result, Set options, Edit SQL commands and PL/SQL.</p></p>
</li><br><br><li class="quesans mb-20">
<p><a class="accordion-trigger ques" id="ques463"><strong>Question 464. What Are Various Joins Used While Writing Subqueries? </strong></a></p>
<p><span class="ans"><strong>Answer :</strong></span><ul>
<li><strong>Self join</strong>-Its a join foreign key of a table references the same table.</li>
<li><strong>Outer Join</strong>--Its a join condition used where One can query all the rows of one of the tables in the join condition even though they don't satisfy the join condition.</li>
<li><strong>Equi-join</strong>-Its a join condition that retrieves rows from one or more tables in which one or more columns in one table are equal to one or more columns in the second table.</li>
</ul></p>
</li><br><br><li class="quesans mb-20">
<p><a class="accordion-trigger ques" id="ques464"><strong>Question 465. What A Select For Update Cursor Represent? </strong></a></p>
<p><span class="ans"><strong>Answer :</strong></span><p>SELECT......FROM......FOR......UPDATE[OF column-reference][NOWAIT].</p>
<p>The processing done in a fetch loop modifies the rows that have been retrieved by the cursor. A convenient way of modifying the rows is done by a method with two parts: the FOR UPDATE clause in the cursor declaration, WHERE CURRENT OF CLAUSE in an UPDATE or declaration statement.</p></p>

<p><span class="ans"><strong>Answer :</strong></span><p>Rename is a permanent name given to a table or column whereas Alias is a temporary name given to a table or column which do not exist once the SQL statement is executed.</p></p>
</li><br><br><li class="quesans mb-20">
<p><a class="accordion-trigger ques" id="ques468"><strong>Question 469. What Is The Difference Between An Implicit &amp; An Explicit Cursor? </strong></a></p>
<p><span class="ans"><strong>Answer :</strong></span><p>only one row. However,queries that return more than one row you must declare an explicit cursor or use a cursor FOR loop. Explicit cursor is a cursor in which the cursor name is explicitly assigned to a SELECT statement via the CURSOR...IS statement. An implicit cursor is used for all SQL statements Declare, Open, Fetch, Close. An explicit cursors are used to process multirow SELECT statements An implicit cursor is used to process INSERT, UPDATE, DELETE and single row SELECT. .INTO statements.</p></p>
</li><br><br><li class="quesans mb-20">
<p><a class="accordion-trigger ques" id="ques469"><strong>Question 470. What Is A Outer Join? </strong></a></p>
<p><span class="ans"><strong>Answer :</strong></span><p><strong>Outer Join:  </strong>Its a join condition used where you can query all the rows of one of the tables in the join condition even though they don’t satisfy the join condition.</p></p>
</li><br><br><li class="quesans mb-20">
<p><a class="accordion-trigger ques" id="ques470"><strong>Question 471. What Is A Cursor? </strong></a></p>
<p><span class="ans"><strong>Answer :</strong></span><p>Oracle uses work area to execute SQL statements and store processing information PL/SQL construct called a cursor lets you name a work area and access its stored information A cursor is a mechanism used to fetch more than one row in a Pl/SQl block.</p></p>
</li><br><br><li class="quesans mb-20">
<p><a class="accordion-trigger ques" id="ques471"><strong>Question 472. What Is The Purpose Of A Cluster? </strong></a></p>
<p><span class="ans"><strong>Answer :</strong></span><p>Oracle does not allow a user to specifically locate tables, since that is a part of the function of the RDBMS. However, for the purpose of increasing performance, oracle allows a developer to create a CLUSTER. A CLUSTER provides a means for storing data from different tables together for faster retrieval than if the table placement were left to the RDBMS.</p></p>
</li><br><br><li class="quesans mb-20">
<p><a class="accordion-trigger ques" id="ques472"><strong>Question 473. What Is Oci. What Are Its Uses? </strong></a></p>
<p><span class="ans"><strong>Answer :</strong></span><p>Oracle Call Interface is a method of accesing database from a 3GL program. Uses No precompiler is required,PL/SQL blocks are executed like other DML statements.  The OCI library provides</p>
<ul>
<li>functions to parse SQL statemets</li>
<li>bind input variables</li>
<li>bind output variables</li>
<li>execute statements</li>
<li>fetch the results</li>
</ul></p>
</li><br><br><li class="quesans mb-20">
<p><a class="accordion-trigger ques" id="ques473"><strong>Question 474. How You Open And Close A Cursor Variable. Why It Is Required? </strong></a></p>
<p><span class="ans"><strong>Answer :</strong></span><p>OPEN cursor variable FOR SELECT...Statement<br/>
CLOSE cursor variable In order to associate a cursor variable with a particular SELECT statement OPEN syntax is used. In order to free the resources used for the query CLOSE statement is used.</p></p>
</li><br><br><li class="quesans mb-20">
<p><a class="accordion-trigger ques" id="ques474"><strong>Question 475. Display Odd/ Even Number Of Records? </strong></a></p>
<p><span class="ans"><strong>Answer :</strong></span><p>Odd number of records:<br/>
select * from emp where (rowid,1) in (select rowid, mod(rownum,2) from emp);<br/>
Output:-<br/>
1<br/>
3<br/>
5<br/>
Even number of records:<br/>
select * from emp where (rowid,0) in (select rowid, mod(rownum,2) from emp)<br/>
Output:-<br/>
2<br/>
4<br/>
6</p></p>

When the where clause of the explicit cursor does not match any rows the %NOTFOUND attribute is set to TRUE instead.</p></p>

<p><a class="accordion-trigger ques" id="ques482"><strong>Question 483. How You Were Passing Cursor Variables In Pl/sql 2.2? </strong></a></p>
<p><span class="ans"><strong>Answer :</strong></span><p>In PL/SQL 2.2 cursor variables cannot be declared in a package.This is because the storage for a cursor variable has to be allocated using Pro*C or OCI with version 2.2, the only means of passing a cursor variable to a PL/SQL block is via bind variable or a procedure parameter.</p></p>
</li><br><br><li class="quesans mb-20">
<p><a class="accordion-trigger ques" id="ques483"><strong>Question 484. When Do You Use Where Clause And When Do You Use Having Clause? </strong></a></p>
<p><span class="ans"><strong>Answer :</strong></span><p>HAVING clause is used when you want to specify a condition for a group function and it is written after GROUP BY clause. The WHERE clause is used when you want to specify a condition for columns, single row functions except group functions and it is written before GROUP BY clause if it is used.</p></p>
</li><br><br><li class="quesans mb-20">
<p><a class="accordion-trigger ques" id="ques484"><strong>Question 485. What Is The Difference Between Procedure And Function? </strong></a></p>
<p><span class="ans"><strong>Answer :</strong></span><p>Functions are named PL/SQL blocks that return a value and can be called with arguments procedure a named block that can be called with parameter.</p>
<p>A procedure all is a PL/SQL statement by itself, while a Function call is called as part of an expression.</p></p>
</li><br><br><li class="quesans mb-20">
<p><a class="accordion-trigger ques" id="ques485"><strong>Question 486. Which Is More Faster - In Or Exists? </strong></a></p>
<p><span class="ans"><strong>Answer :</strong></span><p>EXISTS is more faster than IN because EXISTS returns a Boolean value whereas IN returns a value.</p></p>
</li><br><br><li class="quesans mb-20">

<p><a class="accordion-trigger ques" id="ques487"><strong>Question 488. How Will You Delete Duplicating Rows From A Base Table? </strong></a></p>
<p><span class="ans"><strong>Answer :</strong></span><p>delete from table_name where rowid not in (select max(rowid) from table group by duplicate_values _field_name); or delete duplicate_values_field_name dv from table_name ta where rowid &lt;(select min(rowid) from table_name tb where ta.dv=tb.dv);</p></p>
</li><br><br><li class="quesans mb-20">
<p><a class="accordion-trigger ques" id="ques488"><strong>Question 489. What Is The Difference Between Database Triggers And Form Triggers? </strong></a></p>
<p><span class="ans"><strong>Answer :</strong></span><ul>
<li>Data base trigger(DBT) fires when a DML operation is performed on a data base table. Form trigger(FT) Fires when user presses a key or navigates between fields on the screen.</li>
<li>Can be row level or statement level No distinction between row level and statement level.</li>
<li>Can manipulate data stored in Oracle tables via SQL Can manipulate data in Oracle tables as well as variables in forms.</li>
<li>Can be fired from any session executing the triggering DML statements. Can be fired only from the form that define the trigger.</li>
<li>Can cause other database triggers to fire. Can cause other database triggers to fire, but not other form triggers.</li>
</ul></p>
</li><br><br><li class="quesans mb-20">
<p><a class="accordion-trigger ques" id="ques489"><strong>Question 490. What Is A Cursor For Loop? </strong></a></p>
<p><span class="ans"><strong>Answer :</strong></span><p>Cursor For Loop is a loop where oracle implicitly declares a loop variable, the loop index that of the same record type as the cursor's record.</p></p>
</li><br><br><li class="quesans mb-20">
<p><a class="accordion-trigger ques" id="ques490"><strong>Question 491. How You Will Avoid Duplicating Records In A Query? </strong></a></p>
<p><span class="ans"><strong>Answer :</strong></span><p>By using DISTINCT.</p></p>
</li><br><br><li class="quesans mb-20">
<p><a class="accordion-trigger ques" id="ques491"><strong>Question 492. What Is Difference Between Unique And Primary Key Constraints? </strong></a></p>
<p><span class="ans"><strong>Answer :</strong></span><p>A table can have only one PRIMARY KEY whereas there can be any number of UNIQUE keys. The columns that compose PK are automatically define NOT NULL, whereas a column that compose a UNIQUE is not automatically defined to be mandatory must also specify the column is NOT NULL.</p></p>
</li><br><br><li class="quesans mb-20">
<p><a class="accordion-trigger ques" id="ques492"><strong>Question 493. What Is Use Of A Cursor Variable? How It Is Defined? </strong></a></p>
<p><span class="ans"><strong>Answer :</strong></span><p>A cursor variable is associated with different statements at run time, which can hold different values at run time. Static cursors can only be associated with one run time query. A cursor variable is reference type (like a pointer in C).</p>
<p><strong>Declaring a cursor variable:</strong><br/>
TYPE type_name IS REF CURSOR RETURN return_type type_name is the name of the reference type,return_type is a record type indicating the types of the select list that will eventually be returned by the cursor variable.</p></p>
</li><br><br><li class="quesans mb-20">

<p><span class="ans"><strong>Answer :</strong></span><p>1,000,00.</p></p>

<p><span class="ans"><strong>Answer :</strong></span><p>When ON DELETE CASCADE is specified ORACLE maintains referential integrity by automatically removing dependent foreign key values if a referenced primary or unique key value is removed.</p></p>

<p><a class="accordion-trigger ques" id="ques498"><strong>Question 499. What Is Difference Between Truncate &amp; Delete ? </strong></a></p>
<p><span class="ans"><strong>Answer :</strong></span><p>TRUNCATE commits after deleting entire table i.e., can not be rolled back. Database triggers do not fire on TRUNCATEDELETE allows the filtered deletion. Deleted records can be rolled back or committed. Database triggers fire on DELETE.</p></p>

<p><a class="accordion-trigger ques" id="ques499"><strong>Question 500. What Is A Transaction ? </strong></a></p>

<p><span class="ans"><strong>Answer :</strong></span><p>Sequence name CURRVAL, Sequence name NEXTVAL.It is not possible. Only if you access next value in the session, current value can be accessed.</p></p>

<p><a class="accordion-trigger ques" id="ques505"><strong>Question 506. What Are The Usage Of Savepoints ?value In A Session Before Accessing Next Value ? </strong></a></p>
<p><span class="ans"><strong>Answer :</strong></span><p>SAVEPOINTS are used to subdivide a transaction into smaller parts. It enables rolling back part of a transaction. Maximum of five save points are allowed.</p></p>
</li><br><br><li class="quesans mb-20">

</li><br><br><li class="quesans mb-20">
<p><a class="accordion-trigger ques" id="ques508"><strong>Question 509. How Many Long Columns Are Allowed In A Table ? Is It Possible To Use Long Columns In Where Clause Or Order By ? </strong></a></p>
<p><span class="ans"><strong>Answer :</strong></span><p>Only one LONG column is allowed. It is not possible to use LONG column in WHERE or ORDER BY clause.</p></p>
</li><br><br><li class="quesans mb-20">
<p><a class="accordion-trigger ques" id="ques509"><strong>Question 510. What Is Referential Integrity ? </strong></a></p>
<p><span class="ans"><strong>Answer :</strong></span><p>Maintaining data integrity through a set of rules that restrict the values of one or more columns of the tables based on the values of primary key or unique key of the referenced table.</p></p>
</li><br><br><li class="quesans mb-20">
<p><a class="accordion-trigger ques" id="ques510"><strong>Question 511. What Is A Join ? Explain The Different Types Of Joins ? </strong></a></p>
<p><span class="ans"><strong>Answer :</strong></span><p>Join is a query which retrieves related columns or rows from multiple tables.</p>
<ul>
<li><strong>Self Join</strong> - Joining the table with itself.</li>
<li><strong>Equi Join</strong> - Joining two tables by equating two common columns.</li>
<li><strong>Non-Equi Join</strong> - Joining two tables by equating two common columns.</li>
<li><strong>Outer Join</strong> - Joining two tables in such a way that query can also retrieve rows that do not have corresponding join value in the other table.</li>
</ul></p>
</li><br><br><li class="quesans mb-20">

</li><br><br><li class="quesans mb-20">
<p><a class="accordion-trigger ques" id="ques512"><strong>Question 513. What Is An Integrity Constraint ? </strong></a></p>
<p><span class="ans"><strong>Answer :</strong></span><p>Integrity constraint is a rule that restricts values to a column in a table.</p></p>

</li><br><br><li class="quesans mb-20">
<p><a class="accordion-trigger ques" id="ques515"><strong>Question 516. What Is Cycle/no Cycle In A Sequence ? </strong></a></p>
<p><span class="ans"><strong>Answer :</strong></span><p>CYCLE specifies that the sequence continues to generate values after reaching either maximum or minimum value. After pan ascending sequence reaches its maximum value, it generates its minimum value. After a descending sequence reaches its minimum, it generates its maximum.NO CYCLE specifies that the sequence cannot generate more values after reaching its maximum or minimum value.</p></p>
</li><br><br><li class="quesans mb-20">
<p><a class="accordion-trigger ques" id="ques516"><strong>Question 517. What Is Correlated Sub-query ? </strong></a></p>
<p><span class="ans"><strong>Answer :</strong></span><p>Correlated sub query is a sub query which has reference to the main query.</p></p>

<p><span class="ans"><strong>Answer :</strong></span><p>CHAR pads blank spaces to the maximum length. VARCHAR2 does not pad blank spaces. For CHAR it is 255 and 2000 for VARCHAR2.</p></p>

<p><a class="accordion-trigger ques" id="ques521"><strong>Question 522. Find Out Nth Highest Salary From Emp Table? </strong></a></p>
<p><span class="ans"><strong>Answer :</strong></span><p>SELECT DISTINCT (a.sal) FROM EMP A WHERE &amp;N = (SELECT COUNT (DISTINCT (b.sal)) FROM EMP B WHERE a.sal&lt;=b.sal);<br/>
For E.g.:-<br/>
Enter value for n: 2<br/>
SAL<br/>
---------<br/>
3700</p></p>

<p><a class="accordion-trigger ques" id="ques522"><strong>Question 523. Suppose A Customer Table Is Having Different Columns Like Customer No, Payments. What Will Be The Query To Select Top Three Max Payments? </strong></a></p>
<p><span class="ans"><strong>Answer :</strong></span><p>SELECT customer_no, payments from customer C1<br/>
WHERE 3&lt;=(SELECT COUNT(*) from customer C2<br/>
WHERE C1.payment &lt;= C2.payment)</p></p>

</li><br><br><li class="quesans mb-20">
<p><a class="accordion-trigger ques" id="ques524"><strong>Question 525. How Many Types Of Sql Statements Are There In Oracle? </strong></a></p>
<p><span class="ans"><strong>Answer :</strong></span><p>There are basically 6 types of sql statments.They are</p>
<ul>
<li><strong>Data Definition Language(DDL)</strong> :: The DDL statements define and maintain objects and drop objects.</li>
<li><strong>Data Manipulation Language(DML)</strong> :: The DML statements manipulate database data.</li>
<li><strong>Transaction Control Statements</strong> :: Manage change by DML</li>
<li><strong>Session Control</strong> :: Used to control the properties of current session enabling and disabling roles and changing .e.g. :: Alter Statements, Set Role</li>
<li><strong>System Control Statements</strong> :: Change Properties of Oracle Instance .e.g.:: Alter System</li>
<li><strong>Embedded Sql</strong> :: Incorporate DDL, DML and T.C.S in Programming Language.e.g:: Using the Sql Statements in languages such as 'C', Open, Fetch, execute and close</li>
</ul></p>
</li><br><br><li class="quesans mb-20">
<p><a class="accordion-trigger ques" id="ques525"><strong>Question 526. What Is A Transaction In Oracle ?</strong></a></p>
<p><span class="ans"><strong>Answer :</strong></span><p>A transaction is a Logical unit of work that compromises one or more SQL Statements executed by a single User. According to ANSI, a transaction begins with first executable statement and ends when it is explicitly committed or rolled back.</p></p>
</li><br><br><li class="quesans mb-20">
<p><a class="accordion-trigger ques" id="ques526"><strong>Question 527. What Are Procedure, Functions And Packages ?</strong></a></p>
<p><span class="ans"><strong>Answer :</strong></span><p>Procedures and functions consist of set of PL/SQL statements that are grouped together as a unit to solve a specific problem or perform set of related tasks. Procedures do not Return values while Functions return one.</p>
<p><strong>One Value Packages </strong>:: Packages Provide a method of encapsulating and storing related procedures, functions, variables and other Package Contents</p></p>
</li><br><br><li class="quesans mb-20">
<p><a class="accordion-trigger ques" id="ques527"><strong>Question 528. How Many Integrity Rules Are There And What Are They? </strong></a></p>
<p><span class="ans"><strong>Answer :</strong></span><p>There are Three Integrity Rules. They are as follows ::</p>
<ul>
<li><strong>Entity Integrity Rule</strong> :: The Entity Integrity Rule enforces that the Primary key cannot be Null</li>
<li><strong>Foreign Key Integrity Rule </strong>:: The FKIR denotes that the relationship between the foreign key and the primary key has to be enforced.When there is data in Child Tables the Master tables cannot be deleted.</li>
<li><strong>Business Integrity Rules</strong> :: The Third Intigrity rule is about the complex business processes which cannot be implemented by the above 2 rules.</li>
</ul></p>
</li><br><br><li class="quesans mb-20">
<p><a class="accordion-trigger ques" id="ques528"><strong>Question 529. What Are The Various Master And Detail Relation Ships? </strong></a></p>
<p><span class="ans"><strong>Answer :</strong></span><p>The various Master and Detail Relationship are</p>
<ul>
<li><strong>NonIsolated</strong> :: The Master cannot be deleted when a child is exisiting</li>
<li><strong>Isolated</strong> :: The Master can be deleted when the child is exisiting</li>
<li><strong>Cascading </strong>:: The child gets deleted when the Master is deleted.</li>
</ul></p>
</li><br><br><li class="quesans mb-20">
<p><a class="accordion-trigger ques" id="ques529"><strong>Question 530. What Are The Various Block Coordination Properties? </strong></a></p>
<p><span class="ans"><strong>Answer :</strong></span><p>The various Block Coordination Properties are </p>
<ul>
<li>Immediate Default Setting. The Detail records are shown when the Master Record are shown.</li>
<li>Deffered with Auto Query Oracle Forms defer fetching the detail records until the operator navigates to the detail block.</li>
<li>Deffered with No Auto Query The operator must navigate to the detail block and explicitly execute a query.</li>
</ul></p>
</li><br><br><li class="quesans mb-20">
<p><a class="accordion-trigger ques" id="ques530"><strong>Question 531. What Are Snap Shots And Views?</strong></a></p>
<p><span class="ans"><strong>Answer :</strong></span><p>Snapshots are mirror or replicas of tables. Views are built using the columns from one or more tables. The Single Table View can be updated but the view with multi table cannot be updated.</p></p>
</li><br><br><li class="quesans mb-20">
<p><a class="accordion-trigger ques" id="ques531"><strong>Question 532. What Are The Oops Concepts In Oracle?</strong></a></p>
<p><span class="ans"><strong>Answer :</strong></span><p>Oracle does implement the OOPS concepts. The best example is the Property Classes. We can categorize the properties by setting the visual attributes and then attach the property classes for the objects. OOPS supports the concepts of objects and classes and we can consider the property classes as classes and the items as objects.</p></p>
</li><br><br><li class="quesans mb-20">
<p><a class="accordion-trigger ques" id="ques532"><strong>Question 533. What Is The Difference Between Candidate Key, Unique Key And Primary Key? </strong></a></p>
<p><span class="ans"><strong>Answer :</strong></span><p>Candidate keys are the columns in the table that could be the primary keys and the primary key is the key that has been selected to identify the rows. Unique key is also useful for identifying the distinct rows in the table.</p></p>
</li><br><br><li class="quesans mb-20">
<p><a class="accordion-trigger ques" id="ques533"><strong>Question 534. What Is Concurrency? </strong></a></p>
<p><span class="ans"><strong>Answer :</strong></span><p>Concurrency is allowing simultaneous access of same data by different users. Locks useful for accesing the database are</p>
<ul>
<li><strong>Exclusive:</strong> The exclusive lock is useful for locking the row when an insert,update or delete is being done.This lock should not be applied when we do only select from the row.</li>
<li><strong>Share lock:</strong>  We can do the table as Share_Lock as many share_locks can be put on the same resource.</li>
</ul></p>
</li><br><br><li class="quesans mb-20">
<p><a class="accordion-trigger ques" id="ques534"><strong>Question 535. What Are Previleges And Grants? </strong></a></p>
<p><span class="ans"><strong>Answer :</strong></span><p>Previleges are the right to execute a particulare type of SQL statements.</p>
<p>e.g :: Right to Connect, Right to create, Right to resource Grants are given to the objects so that the object might be accessed accordingly.</p>
<p>The grant has to be given by the owner of the object.</p></p>
</li><br><br><li class="quesans mb-20">
<p><a class="accordion-trigger ques" id="ques535"><strong>Question 536. Physical Storage Of The Data? </strong></a></p>
<p><span class="ans"><strong>Answer :</strong></span><p>The finest level of granularity of the data base are the data blocks.<br/>
Data Block :: One Data Block correspond to specific number of physical database space.<br/>
Extent :: Extent is the number of specific number of contigious data blocks.<br/>
Segments :: Set of Extents allocated for Extents. There are three types of Segments<br/>
a) Data Segment :: Non Clustered Table has data segment data of every table is stored in cluster data segment.<br/>
b) Index Segment :: Each Index has index segment that stores data.<br/>
c) Roll Back Segment :: Temporarily store 'undo' information</p></p>
</li><br><br><li class="quesans mb-20">
<p><a class="accordion-trigger ques" id="ques536"><strong>Question 537. What Are The Pct Free And Pct Used?</strong></a></p>
<p><span class="ans"><strong>Answer :</strong></span><p>Pct Free is used to denote the percentage of the free space that is to be left when creating a table. Similarly Pct Used is used to denote the percentage of the used space that is to be used when creating a table<br/>
eg.:: Pctfree 20, Pctused 40</p></p>
</li><br><br><li class="quesans mb-20">
<p><a class="accordion-trigger ques" id="ques537"><strong>Question 538. What Is Row Chaining?</strong></a></p>
<p><span class="ans"><strong>Answer :</strong></span><p>The data of a row in a table may not be able to fit the same data block.Data for row is stored in a chain of data blocks .</p></p>
</li><br><br><li class="quesans mb-20">
<p><a class="accordion-trigger ques" id="ques538"><strong>Question 539. What Is A 2 Phase Commit?</strong></a></p>
<p><span class="ans"><strong>Answer :</strong></span><p>Two Phase commit is used in distributed data base systems. This is useful to maintain the integrity of the database so that all the users see the same values. It contains DML statements or Remote Procedural calls that reference a remote object. There are basically 2 phases in a 2 phase commit.</p>
<ul>
<li><strong>Prepare Phase</strong> :: Global coordinator asks participants to prepare</li>
<li><strong>Commit Phase</strong> :: Commit all participants to coordinator to Prepared, Read only or abort Reply</li>
</ul></p>
</li><br><br><li class="quesans mb-20">
<p><a class="accordion-trigger ques" id="ques539"><strong>Question 540. What Is The Difference Between Deleting And Truncating Of Tables? </strong></a></p>
<p><span class="ans"><strong>Answer :</strong></span><p>Deleting a table will not remove the rows from the table but entry is there in the database dictionary and it can be retrieved But truncating a table deletes it completely and it cannot be retrieved.</p></p>
</li><br><br><li class="quesans mb-20">
<p><a class="accordion-trigger ques" id="ques540"><strong>Question 541. What Are Mutating Tables?</strong></a></p>
<p><span class="ans"><strong>Answer :</strong></span><p>When a table is in state of transition it is said to be mutating.</p>
<p>eg :: If a row has been deleted then the table is said to be mutating and no operations can be done on the table except select.</p></p>
</li><br><br><li class="quesans mb-20">
<p><a class="accordion-trigger ques" id="ques541"><strong>Question 542. What Are Codd Rules? </strong></a></p>
<p><span class="ans"><strong>Answer :</strong></span><p>Codd Rules describe the ideal nature of a RDBMS. No RDBMS satisfies all the 12 codd rules and Oracle Satisfies 11 of the 12 rules and is the only Rdbms to satisfy the maximum number of rules.</p></p>
</li><br><br><li class="quesans mb-20">
<p><a class="accordion-trigger ques" id="ques542"><strong>Question 543. What Is Normalisation?</strong></a></p>
<p><span class="ans"><strong>Answer :</strong></span><p>Normalisation is the process of organising the tables to remove the redundancy.There are mainly 5 Normalisation rules.</p>
<ul>
<li><strong>1 Normal Form</strong> :: A table is said to be in 1st Normal Form when the attributes are atomic.</li>
<li><strong>2 Normal Form</strong> :: A table is said to be in 2nd Normal Form when all the candidate keys are dependant on the primary key.</li>
<li><strong>3rd Normal Form</strong> :: A table is said to be third Normal form when it is not dependant transitively.</li>
</ul></p>
</li><br><br><li class="quesans mb-20">
<p><a class="accordion-trigger ques" id="ques543"><strong>Question 544. What Is The Difference Between A Post Query And A Pre Query?</strong></a></p>
<p><span class="ans"><strong>Answer :</strong></span><p>A post query will fire for every row that is fetched but the pre query will fire only once.</p></p>
</li><br><br><li class="quesans mb-20">
<p><a class="accordion-trigger ques" id="ques544"><strong>Question 545. Can We Delete The Duplicate Rows In The Table?</strong></a></p>
<p><span class="ans"><strong>Answer :</strong></span><p>Yes. We can delete the duplicate rows in the table by using the Rowid.</p></p>
</li><br><br><li class="quesans mb-20">
<p><a class="accordion-trigger ques" id="ques545"><strong>Question 546. Can U Disable Database Trigger? How? </strong></a></p>
<p><span class="ans"><strong>Answer :</strong></span><p>Yes. With respect to table<br/>
ALTER TABLE TABLE<br/>
[[ DISABLE all_trigger ]]</p></p>
</li><br><br><li class="quesans mb-20">
<p><a class="accordion-trigger ques" id="ques546"><strong>Question 547. What Is Pseudo Columns ? Name Them? </strong></a></p>
<p><span class="ans"><strong>Answer :</strong></span><p>A pseudocolumn behaves like a table column, but is not actually stored in the table. You can select from pseudocolumns, but you cannot insert, update, or delete their values. This section describes these pseudocolumns:</p>
<ul>
<li>CURRVAL</li>
<li>NEXTVAL</li>
<li>LEVEL</li>
<li>ROWID</li>
<li>ROWNUM</li>
</ul></p>

<p><a class="accordion-trigger ques" id="ques555"><strong>Question 556. What Are Object Groups? </strong></a></p>

</li><br><br><li class="quesans mb-20">
<p><a class="accordion-trigger ques" id="ques556"><strong>Question 557. What Are Referenced Objects? </strong></a></p>
<p><span class="ans"><strong>Answer :</strong></span><p>Referencing allows you to create objects that inherit their functionality and appearance from other objects. Referencing an object is similar to copying an object, except that the resulting reference object maintains a link to its source object. A reference object automatically inherits any changes that have been made to the source object when you open or regenerate the module that contains the reference object.</p></p>

Yes . All type of triggers .</p></p>

<p><span class="ans"><strong>Answer :</strong></span><p>Item level trigger fires , If item level trigger fires, property level trigger won't fire. Triggers at the lowest level are always given the first preference. The item level trigger fires first and then the block and then the Form level trigger.</p></p>

When Mouse Navigate is set to False, Oracle Forms does not perform navigation (and the resulting validation) to move to the item when an operator activates the item with the mouse.</p></p>

<p><a class="accordion-trigger ques" id="ques569"><strong>Question 570. What Are User-exits? </strong></a></p>
<p><span class="ans"><strong>Answer :</strong></span><p>A user exit is a C subroutine written by you and called by Oracle Forms to do special-purpose processing. You can embed SQL statements and PL/SQL blocks in your user exit, then precompile it as you would a host program.</p>
<p>When called by an Oracle Forms V3 trigger, the user exit runs, then returns a status code to Oracle Forms. Your exit can display messages on the Oracle Forms status line, get and set field values, do high-speed computations and table lookups, and manipulate Oracle data.</p></p>
</li><br><br><li class="quesans mb-20">
<p><a class="accordion-trigger ques" id="ques570"><strong>Question 571. Can You Pass Values To-and-fro From Foreign Function? How? </strong></a></p>
<p><span class="ans"><strong>Answer :</strong></span><p>Yes . You obtain a return value from a foreign function by assigning the return value to an Oracle Forms variable or item. Make sure that the Oracle Forms variable or item is the same data type as the return value from the foreign function.</p>
<p>After assigning an Oracle Forms variable or item value to a PL/SQL variable, pass the PL/SQL variable as a parameter value in the PL/SQL interface of the foreign function. The PL/SQL variable that is passed as a parameter must be a valid PL/SQL data type; it must also be the appropriate parameter type as defined in the PL/SQL interface.</p></p>
</li><br><br><li class="quesans mb-20">
<p><a class="accordion-trigger ques" id="ques571"><strong>Question 572. What Is Iapxtb Structure ? </strong></a></p>
<p><span class="ans"><strong>Answer :</strong></span><p>The entries of Pro * C and user exits and the form which simulate the proc or user_exit are stored in IAPXTB table in d/b.</p></p>

<p><a class="accordion-trigger ques" id="ques580"><strong>Question 581. What Is Ole Automation? </strong></a></p>
<p><span class="ans"><strong>Answer :</strong></span><p>OLE automation allows an OLE server application to expose a set of commands and functions that can be invoked from an OLE container application. OLE automation provides a way for an OLE container application to use the features of an OLE server application to manipulate an OLE object from the OLE container environment. (FORMS_OLE).</p></p>
</li><br><br><li class="quesans mb-20">
<p><a class="accordion-trigger ques" id="ques581"><strong>Question 582. What Does Invoke Built-in Do?</strong></a></p>
<p><span class="ans"><strong>Answer :</strong></span><p>This procedure invokes a method.</p>
<p><em><strong>Syntax:</strong></em></p>
<pre>
PROCEDURE OLE2.INVOKE
(object obj_type,
method VARCHAR2,
list list_type := 0);
</pre>
<p><em><strong>Parameters:</strong></em></p>
<ul>
<li>object Is an OLE2 Automation Object.</li>
<li>method Is a method (procedure) of the OLE2 object.</li>
<li>list Is the name of an argument list assigned to the OLE2.CREATE_ARGLIST function.</li>
</ul></p>
</li><br><br><li class="quesans mb-20">
<p><a class="accordion-trigger ques" id="ques582"><strong>Question 583. What Is Call Form Stack? </strong></a></p>
