<p><a class="accordion-trigger ques" id="ques588"><strong>Question 589. What Is Log Switch ? </strong></a></p>
<p><span class="ans"><strong>Answer :</strong></span><p>The point at which ORACLE ends writing to one online redo log file and begins writing to another is called a log switch.</p></p>
</li><br><br><li class="quesans mb-20">
<p><a class="accordion-trigger ques" id="ques589"><strong>Question 590. What Is On-line Redo Log? </strong></a></p>
<p><span class="ans"><strong>Answer :</strong></span><p>The On-line Redo Log is a set of two or more on-line redo files that record all committed changes made to the database. Whenever a transaction is committed, the corresponding redo entries temporarily stores in redo log buffers of the SGA are written to an on-line redo log file by the background process LGWR. The on-line redo log files are used in cyclical fashion.</p></p>
</li><br><br><li class="quesans mb-20">
<p><a class="accordion-trigger ques" id="ques590"><strong>Question 591. Which Parameter Specified In The Default Storage Clause Of Create Tablespace Cannot Be Altered After Creating The Tablespace? </strong></a></p>
<p><span class="ans"><strong>Answer :</strong></span><p>All the default storage parameters defined for the tablespace can be changed using the ALTER TABLESPACE command. When objects are created their INITIAL and MINEXTENS values cannot be changed.</p></p>
</li><br><br><li class="quesans mb-20">
<p><a class="accordion-trigger ques" id="ques591"><strong>Question 592. What Are The Steps Involved In Database Startup? </strong></a></p>
<p><span class="ans"><strong>Answer :</strong></span><p>Start an instance, Mount the Database and Open the Database. </p>
<p>Rolling forward to recover data that has not been recorded in data files, yet has been recorded in the on-line redo log, including the contents of rollback segments. Rolling back transactions that have been explicitly rolled back or have not been committed as indicated by the rollback segments regenerated in step a. Releasing any resources (locks) held by transactions in process at the time of the failure. Resolving any pending distributed transactions undergoing a two-phase commit at the time of the instance failure.</p></p>
</li><br><br><li class="quesans mb-20">
<p><a class="accordion-trigger ques" id="ques592"><strong>Question 593. Can Full Backup Be Performed When The Database Is Open? </strong></a></p>
<p><span class="ans"><strong>Answer :</strong></span><p>No.</p></p>
</li><br><br><li class="quesans mb-20">
<p><a class="accordion-trigger ques" id="ques593"><strong>Question 594. What Are The Different Modes Of Mounting A Database With The Parallel Server? </strong></a></p>
<p><span class="ans"><strong>Answer :</strong></span><p>Exclusive Mode If the first instance that mounts a database does so in exclusive mode, only that Instance can mount the database.</p>
<p>Parallel Mode If the first instance that mounts a database is started in parallel mode, other instances that are started in parallel mode can also mount the database.</p></p>
</li><br><br><li class="quesans mb-20">
<p><a class="accordion-trigger ques" id="ques594"><strong>Question 595. What Are The Advantages Of Operating A Database In Archivelog Mode Over Operating It In No Archivelog Mode ? </strong></a></p>
<p><span class="ans"><strong>Answer :</strong></span><p>Complete database recovery from disk failure is possible only in ARCHIVELOG mode. Online database backup is possible only in ARCHIVELOG mode.</p></p>
</li><br><br><li class="quesans mb-20">
<p><a class="accordion-trigger ques" id="ques595"><strong>Question 596. What Are The Steps Involved In Database Shutdown ? </strong></a></p>
<p><span class="ans"><strong>Answer :</strong></span><p>Close the Database, Dismount the Database and Shutdown the Instance.</p></p>
</li><br><br><li class="quesans mb-20">
<p><a class="accordion-trigger ques" id="ques596"><strong>Question 597. What Is Archived Redo Log ? </strong></a></p>
<p><span class="ans"><strong>Answer :</strong></span><p>Archived Redo Log consists of Redo Log files that have archived before being reused.</p></p>
</li><br><br><li class="quesans mb-20">
<p><a class="accordion-trigger ques" id="ques597"><strong>Question 598. What Is Restricted Mode Of Instance Startup ? </strong></a></p>
<p><span class="ans"><strong>Answer :</strong></span><p>An instance can be started in (or later altered to be in) restricted mode so that when the database is open connections are limited only to those whose user accounts have been granted the RESTRICTED SESSION system privilege.</p></p>

</li><br><br><li class="quesans mb-20">
<p><a class="accordion-trigger ques" id="ques611"><strong>Question 612. What Is A Segment ? </strong></a></p>
<p><span class="ans"><strong>Answer :</strong></span><p>A segment is a set of extents allocated for a certain logical structure.</p></p>
</li><br><br><li class="quesans mb-20">
<p><a class="accordion-trigger ques" id="ques612"><strong>Question 613. Describe Referential Integrity ? </strong></a></p>
<p><span class="ans"><strong>Answer :</strong></span><p>A rule defined on a column (or set of columns) in one table that allows the insert or update of a row only if the value for the column or set of columns (the dependent value) matches a value in a column of a related table (the referenced value). It also specifies the type of data manipulation allowed on referenced data and the action to be performed on dependent data as a result of any action on referenced data.</p></p>
</li><br><br><li class="quesans mb-20">
<p><a class="accordion-trigger ques" id="ques613"><strong>Question 614. What Is Hash Cluster ? </strong></a></p>
<p><span class="ans"><strong>Answer :</strong></span><p>A row is stored in a hash cluster based on the result of applying a hash function to the row's cluster key value. All rows with the same hash key value are stores together on disk.</p></p>
</li><br><br><li class="quesans mb-20">
<p><a class="accordion-trigger ques" id="ques614"><strong>Question 615. What Is A Private Synonyms ? </strong></a></p>
<p><span class="ans"><strong>Answer :</strong></span><p>A Private Synonyms can be accessed only by the owner.</p></p>
</li><br><br><li class="quesans mb-20">
<p><a class="accordion-trigger ques" id="ques615"><strong>Question 616. What Is Database Link ? </strong></a></p>
<p><span class="ans"><strong>Answer :</strong></span><p>A database link is a named object that describes a "path" from one database to another.</p></p>
</li><br><br><li class="quesans mb-20">
<p><a class="accordion-trigger ques" id="ques616"><strong>Question 617. What Is Index Cluster? </strong></a></p>
<p><span class="ans"><strong>Answer :</strong></span><p>A cluster with an index on the cluster key.</p></p>
</li><br><br><li class="quesans mb-20">
<p><a class="accordion-trigger ques" id="ques617"><strong>Question 618. What Is Hash Cluster? </strong></a></p>
<p><span class="ans"><strong>Answer :</strong></span><p>A row is stored in a hash cluster based on the result of applying a hash function to the row's cluster key value. All rows with the same hash key value are stores together on disk.</p></p>
</li><br><br><li class="quesans mb-20">
<p><a class="accordion-trigger ques" id="ques618"><strong>Question 619. When Can Hash Cluster Used? </strong></a></p>
<p><span class="ans"><strong>Answer :</strong></span><p>Hash clusters are better choice when a table is often queried with equality queries. For such queries the specified cluster key value is hashed. The resulting hash key value points directly to the area on disk that stores the specified rows.</p></p>
</li><br><br><li class="quesans mb-20">
<p><a class="accordion-trigger ques" id="ques619"><strong>Question 620. What Are The Types Of Database Links? </strong></a></p>
<p><span class="ans"><strong>Answer :</strong></span><p>Private database link, public database link &amp; network database link.</p></p>
</li><br><br><li class="quesans mb-20">
<p><a class="accordion-trigger ques" id="ques620"><strong>Question 621. What Is Private Database Link? </strong></a></p>
<p><span class="ans"><strong>Answer :</strong></span><p>Private database link is created on behalf of a specific user. A private database link can be used only when the owner of the link specifies a global object name in a SQL statement or in the definition of the owner's views or procedures.</p></p>
</li><br><br><li class="quesans mb-20">
<p><a class="accordion-trigger ques" id="ques621"><strong>Question 622. What Is Public Database Link? </strong></a></p>
<p><span class="ans"><strong>Answer :</strong></span><p>Public database link is created for the special user group PUBLIC. A public database link can be used when any user in the associated database specifies a global object name in a SQL statement or object definition.</p></p>
</li><br><br><li class="quesans mb-20">
<p><a class="accordion-trigger ques" id="ques622"><strong>Question 623. What Is Network Database Link? </strong></a></p>
<p><span class="ans"><strong>Answer :</strong></span><p>Network database link is created and managed by a network domain service. A network database link can be used when any user of any database in the network specifies a global object name in a SQL statement or object definition.</p></p>
</li><br><br><li class="quesans mb-20">
<p><a class="accordion-trigger ques" id="ques623"><strong>Question 624. What Is Data Block? </strong></a></p>
<p><span class="ans"><strong>Answer :</strong></span><p>Oracle database's data is stored in data blocks. One data block corresponds to a specific number of bytes of physical database space on disk.</p></p>
</li><br><br><li class="quesans mb-20">
<p><a class="accordion-trigger ques" id="ques624"><strong>Question 625. How To Define Data Block Size? </strong></a></p>
<p><span class="ans"><strong>Answer :</strong></span><p>A data block size is specified for each Oracle database when the database is created. A database users and allocated free database space in Oracle data blocks. Block size is specified in init. ora file and cannot be changed latter.</p></p>
</li><br><br><li class="quesans mb-20">
<p><a class="accordion-trigger ques" id="ques625"><strong>Question 626. What Is An Extent? </strong></a></p>
<p><span class="ans"><strong>Answer :</strong></span><p>An extent is a specific number of contiguous data blocks, obtained in a single allocation and used to store a specific type of information.</p></p>
</li><br><br><li class="quesans mb-20">
<p><a class="accordion-trigger ques" id="ques626"><strong>Question 627. What Are The Different Types Of Segments?</strong></a></p>
<p><span class="ans"><strong>Answer :</strong></span><p>Data segment, index segment, rollback segment and temporary segment.</p></p>
</li><br><br><li class="quesans mb-20">
<p><a class="accordion-trigger ques" id="ques627"><strong>Question 628. What Is An Index Segment? </strong></a></p>
<p><span class="ans"><strong>Answer :</strong></span><p>Each index has an index segment that stores all of its data.</p></p>
</li><br><br><li class="quesans mb-20">
<p><a class="accordion-trigger ques" id="ques628"><strong>Question 629. What Is Rollback Segment? </strong></a></p>
<p><span class="ans"><strong>Answer :</strong></span><p>A database contains one or more rollback segments to temporarily store "undo" information.</p></p>
</li><br><br><li class="quesans mb-20">
<p><a class="accordion-trigger ques" id="ques629"><strong>Question 630. What Are The Uses Of Rollback Segment? </strong></a></p>
<p><span class="ans"><strong>Answer :</strong></span><p>To generate read-consistent database information during database recovery and to rollback uncommitted transactions by the users.</p></p>
</li><br><br><li class="quesans mb-20">
<p><a class="accordion-trigger ques" id="ques630"><strong>Question 631. What Is A Temporary Segment? </strong></a></p>
<p><span class="ans"><strong>Answer :</strong></span><p>Temporary segments are created by Oracle when a SQL statement needs a temporary work area to complete execution. When the statement finishes execution, the temporary segment extents are released to the system for future use.</p></p>
</li><br><br><li class="quesans mb-20">
<p><a class="accordion-trigger ques" id="ques631"><strong>Question 632. What Is A Datafile? </strong></a></p>
<p><span class="ans"><strong>Answer :</strong></span><p>Every Oracle database has one or more physical data files. A database's data files contain all the database data. The data of logical database structures such as tables and indexes is physically stored in the data files allocated for a database.</p></p>
</li><br><br><li class="quesans mb-20">
<p><a class="accordion-trigger ques" id="ques632"><strong>Question 633. What Are The Characteristics Of Data Files? </strong></a></p>
<p><span class="ans"><strong>Answer :</strong></span><p>A data file can be associated with only one database. Once created a data file can't change size. One or more data files form a logical unit of database storage called a tablespace.</p></p>
</li><br><br><li class="quesans mb-20">
<p><a class="accordion-trigger ques" id="ques633"><strong>Question 634. What Is A Redo Log? </strong></a></p>
<p><span class="ans"><strong>Answer :</strong></span><p>The set of redo log files for a database is collectively known as the database redo log.</p></p>
</li><br><br><li class="quesans mb-20">
<p><a class="accordion-trigger ques" id="ques634"><strong>Question 635. What Is The Function Of Redo Log? </strong></a></p>
<p><span class="ans"><strong>Answer :</strong></span><p>The primary function of the redo log is to record all changes made to data.</p></p>
</li><br><br><li class="quesans mb-20">
<p><a class="accordion-trigger ques" id="ques635"><strong>Question 636. What Is The Use Of Redo Log Information? </strong></a></p>
<p><span class="ans"><strong>Answer :</strong></span><p>The information in a redo log file is used only to recover the database from a system or media failure prevents database data from being written to a database's data files.</p></p>
</li><br><br><li class="quesans mb-20">
<p><a class="accordion-trigger ques" id="ques636"><strong>Question 637. What Does A Control File Contains? </strong></a></p>
<p><span class="ans"><strong>Answer :</strong></span><ul>
<li>Database name</li>
<li>Names and locations of a database's files and redolog files.</li>
<li>Time stamp of database creation.</li>
</ul></p>
</li><br><br><li class="quesans mb-20">
<p><a class="accordion-trigger ques" id="ques637"><strong>Question 638. What Is The Use Of Control File? </strong></a></p>
<p><span class="ans"><strong>Answer :</strong></span><p>When an instance of an Oracle database is started, its control file is used to identify the database and redo log files that must be opened for database operation to proceed. It is also used in database recovery.</p></p>
</li><br><br><li class="quesans mb-20">
<p><a class="accordion-trigger ques" id="ques638"><strong>Question 639. Is It Possible To Split The Print Reviewer Into More Than One Region? </strong></a></p>
<p><span class="ans"><strong>Answer :</strong></span><p>Yes.</p></p>
</li><br><br><li class="quesans mb-20">

<p><span class="ans"><strong>Answer :</strong></span><p>Yes.</p></p>
</li><br><br><li class="quesans mb-20">
<p><a class="accordion-trigger ques" id="ques640"><strong>Question 641. For A Field In A Repeating Frame, Can The Source Come From The Column Which Does Not Exist In The Data Group Which Forms The Base For The Frame? </strong></a></p>

</li><br><br><li class="quesans mb-20">
<p><a class="accordion-trigger ques" id="ques647"><strong>Question 648. When A Form Is Invoked With Call_form, Does Oracle Forms Issues A Save Point? </strong></a></p>
<p><span class="ans"><strong>Answer :</strong></span><p>Yes.</p></p>
</li><br><br><li class="quesans mb-20">
<p><a class="accordion-trigger ques" id="ques648"><strong>Question 649. Explain The Difference Between A Hot Backup And A Cold Backup And The Benefits Associated With Each?</strong></a></p>
<p><span class="ans"><strong>Answer :</strong></span><p>A hot backup is basically taking a backup of the database while it is still up and running and it must be in archive log mode. A cold backup is taking a backup of the database while it is shut down and does not require being in archive log mode. The benefit of taking a hot backup is that the database is still available for use while the backup is occurring and you can recover the database to any point in time. The benefit of taking a cold backup is that it is typically easier to administer the backup and recovery process. In addition, since you are taking cold backups the database does not require being in archive log mode and thus there will be a slight performance gain as the database is not cutting archive logs to disk.</p></p>
</li><br><br><li class="quesans mb-20">
<p><a class="accordion-trigger ques" id="ques649"><strong>Question 650. You Have Just Had To Restore From Backup And Do Not Have Any Control Files. How Would You Go About Bringing Up This Database? </strong></a></p>
<p><span class="ans"><strong>Answer :</strong></span><p>I would create a text based backup control file, stipulating where on disk all the data files where and then issue the recover command with the using backup control file clause.</p></p>
</li><br><br><li class="quesans mb-20">
<p><a class="accordion-trigger ques" id="ques650"><strong>Question 651. How Do You Switch From An Init.ora File To A Spfile? </strong></a></p>
<p><span class="ans"><strong>Answer :</strong></span><p>Issue the create spfile from pfile command.</p></p>
</li><br><br><li class="quesans mb-20">
<p><a class="accordion-trigger ques" id="ques651"><strong>Question 652. Explain The Difference Between A Data Block, An Extent And A Segment?</strong></a></p>
<p><span class="ans"><strong>Answer :</strong></span><p>A data block is the smallest unit of logical storage for a database object. As objects grow they take chunks of additional storage that are composed of contiguous data blocks. These groupings of contiguous data blocks are called extents. All the extents that an object takes when grouped together are considered the segment of the database object.</p></p>
</li><br><br><li class="quesans mb-20">
<p><a class="accordion-trigger ques" id="ques652"><strong>Question 653. Give Two Examples Of How You Might Determine The Structure Of The Table Dept?</strong></a></p>
<p><span class="ans"><strong>Answer :</strong></span><p>Use the describe command or use the dbms_metadata. get_ddl package.</p></p>
</li><br><br><li class="quesans mb-20">
<p><a class="accordion-trigger ques" id="ques653"><strong>Question 654. Where Would You Look For Errors From The Database Engine? </strong></a></p>
<p><span class="ans"><strong>Answer :</strong></span><p>In the alert log.</p></p>
</li><br><br><li class="quesans mb-20">
<p><a class="accordion-trigger ques" id="ques654"><strong>Question 655. Compare And Contrast Truncate And Delete For A Table?</strong></a></p>
<p><span class="ans"><strong>Answer :</strong></span><p>Both the truncate and delete command have the desired outcome of getting rid of all the rows in a table. The difference between the two is that the truncate command is a DDL operation and just moves the high water mark and produces a now rollback. The delete command, on the other hand, is a DML operation, which will produce a rollback and thus take longer to complete.</p></p>
</li><br><br><li class="quesans mb-20">
<p><a class="accordion-trigger ques" id="ques655"><strong>Question 656. Give The Reasoning Behind Using An Index?</strong></a></p>
<p><span class="ans"><strong>Answer :</strong></span><p>Faster access to data blocks in a table.</p></p>
</li><br><br><li class="quesans mb-20">
<p><a class="accordion-trigger ques" id="ques656"><strong>Question 657. Give The Two Types Of Tables Involved In Producing A Star Schema And The Type Of Data They Hold?</strong></a></p>
<p><span class="ans"><strong>Answer :</strong></span><p>Fact tables and dimension tables. A fact table contains measurements while dimension tables will contain data that will help describe the fact tables.</p></p>
</li><br><br><li class="quesans mb-20">
<p><a class="accordion-trigger ques" id="ques657"><strong>Question 658. What Type Of Index Should You Use On A Fact Table? </strong></a></p>
<p><span class="ans"><strong>Answer :</strong></span><p>A Bitmap index.</p></p>
</li><br><br><li class="quesans mb-20">
<p><a class="accordion-trigger ques" id="ques658"><strong>Question 659. Give Two Examples Of Referential Integrity Constraints?</strong></a></p>
<p><span class="ans"><strong>Answer :</strong></span><p>A primary key and a foreign key.</p></p>
</li><br><br><li class="quesans mb-20">
<p><a class="accordion-trigger ques" id="ques659"><strong>Question 660. A Table Is Classified As A Parent Table And You Want To Drop And Re-create It. How Would You Do This Without Affecting The Children Tables? </strong></a></p>
<p><span class="ans"><strong>Answer :</strong></span><p>Disable the foreign key constraint to the parent, drop the table, re-create the table, enable the foreign key constraint.</p></p>
</li><br><br><li class="quesans mb-20">
<p><a class="accordion-trigger ques" id="ques660"><strong>Question 661. Explain The Difference Between Archivelog Mode And Noarchivelog Mode And The Benefits And Disadvantages To Each?</strong></a></p>
<p><span class="ans"><strong>Answer :</strong></span><p>ARCHIVELOG mode is a mode that you can put the database in for creating a backup of all transactions that have occurred in the database so that you can recover to any point in time. </p>
<p>NOARCHIVELOG mode is basically the absence of ARCHIVELOG mode and has the disadvantage of not being able to recover to any point in time. NOARCHIVELOG mode does have the advantage of not having to write transactions to an archive log and thus increases the performance of the database slightly.</p></p>
</li><br><br><li class="quesans mb-20">
<p><a class="accordion-trigger ques" id="ques661"><strong>Question 662. What Command Would You Use To Create A Backup Control File?</strong></a></p>
<p><span class="ans"><strong>Answer :</strong></span><p>Alter database backup control file to trace.</p></p>
</li><br><br><li class="quesans mb-20">
<p><a class="accordion-trigger ques" id="ques662"><strong>Question 663. Give The Stages Of Instance Startup To A Usable State Where Normal Users May Access It?</strong></a></p>
<p><span class="ans"><strong>Answer :</strong></span><p><em><strong>STARTUP NOMOUNT:</strong></em>  Instance startup.</p>
<p><em><strong>STARTUP MOUNT: </strong></em>The database is mounted.</p>
<p><em><strong>STARTUP OPEN:</strong></em> The database is opened.</p></p>
</li><br><br><li class="quesans mb-20">
<p><a class="accordion-trigger ques" id="ques663"><strong>Question 664. What Column Differentiates The V$ Views To The Gv$ Views And How? </strong></a></p>
<p><span class="ans"><strong>Answer :</strong></span><p>The INST_ID column which indicates the instance in a RAC environment the information came from.</p></p>
</li><br><br><li class="quesans mb-20">
<p><a class="accordion-trigger ques" id="ques664"><strong>Question 665. How Would You Go About Increasing The Buffer Cache Hit Ratio? </strong></a></p>
<p><span class="ans"><strong>Answer :</strong></span><p>Use the buffer cache advisory over a given workload and then query the v$db_cache_advice table. If a change was necessary then I would use the alter system set db_cache_size command.</p></p>
</li><br><br><li class="quesans mb-20">
<p><a class="accordion-trigger ques" id="ques665"><strong>Question 666. Explain An Ora-01555? </strong></a></p>
<p><span class="ans"><strong>Answer :</strong></span><p>You get this error when you get a snapshot too old within rollback. It can usually be solved by increasing the undo retention or increasing the size of rollbacks. You should also look at the logic involved in the application getting the error message.</p></p>
</li><br><br><li class="quesans mb-20">
<p><a class="accordion-trigger ques" id="ques666"><strong>Question 667. Explain The Difference Between $oracle_home And $oracle_base?</strong></a></p>
<p><span class="ans"><strong>Answer :</strong></span><p>ORACLE_BASE is the root directory for oracle. ORACLE_HOME located beneath. ORACLE_BASE is where the oracle products reside.</p></p>
</li><br><br><li class="quesans mb-20">
<p><a class="accordion-trigger ques" id="ques667"><strong>Question 668. How Would You Determine The Time Zone Under Which A Database Was Operating? </strong></a></p>
<p><span class="ans"><strong>Answer :</strong></span><p>select DBTIMEZONE from dual;</p></p>
</li><br><br><li class="quesans mb-20">
<p><a class="accordion-trigger ques" id="ques668"><strong>Question 669. Explain The Use Of Setting Global_names Equal To True?</strong></a></p>
<p><span class="ans"><strong>Answer :</strong></span><p>Setting GLOBAL_NAMES dictates how you might connect to a database. This variable is either TRUE or FALSE and if it is set to TRUE it enforces database links to have the same name as the remote database to which they are linking.</p></p>
</li><br><br><li class="quesans mb-20">
<p><a class="accordion-trigger ques" id="ques669"><strong>Question 670. What Command Would You Use To Encrypt A Pl/sql Application?</strong></a></p>
<p><span class="ans"><strong>Answer :</strong></span><p>WRAP.</p></p>
</li><br><br><li class="quesans mb-20">
<p><a class="accordion-trigger ques" id="ques670"><strong>Question 671. Explain The Difference Between A Function, Procedure And Package?</strong></a></p>
<p><span class="ans"><strong>Answer :</strong></span><p>A function and procedure are the same in that they are intended to be a collection of PL/SQL code that carries a single task. While a procedure does not have to return any values to the calling application, a function will return a single value. A package on the other hand is a collection of functions and procedures that are grouped together based on their commonality to a business function or application.</p></p>
</li><br><br><li class="quesans mb-20">
<p><a class="accordion-trigger ques" id="ques671"><strong>Question 672. Explain The Use Of Table Functions?</strong></a></p>
<p><span class="ans"><strong>Answer :</strong></span><p>Table functions are designed to return a set of rows through PL/SQL logic but are intended to be used as a normal table or view in a SQL statement. They are also used to pipeline information in an ETL process.</p></p>
</li><br><br><li class="quesans mb-20">
<p><a class="accordion-trigger ques" id="ques672"><strong>Question 673. Name Three Advisory Statistics You Can Collect?</strong></a></p>
<p><span class="ans"><strong>Answer :</strong></span><p>Buffer Cache Advice, Segment Level Statistics, &amp; Timed Statistics.</p></p>
</li><br><br><li class="quesans mb-20">

</li><br><br><li class="quesans mb-20">
<p><a class="accordion-trigger ques" id="ques674"><strong>Question 675. Explain Materialized Views And How They Are Used?</strong></a></p>
<p><span class="ans"><strong>Answer :</strong></span><p>Materialized views are objects that are reduced sets of information that have been summarized, grouped, or aggregated from base tables. They are typically used in data warehouse or decision support systems.</p></p>
</li><br><br><li class="quesans mb-20">

<p><a class="accordion-trigger ques" id="ques676"><strong>Question 677. What Background Process Refreshes Materialized Views? </strong></a></p>

</li><br><br><li class="quesans mb-20">
<p><a class="accordion-trigger ques" id="ques677"><strong>Question 678. How Would You Determine What Sessions Are Connected And What Resources They Are Waiting For? </strong></a></p>
<p><span class="ans"><strong>Answer :</strong></span><p>Use of V$SESSION and V$SESSION_WAIT.</p></p>
</li><br><br><li class="quesans mb-20">
<p><a class="accordion-trigger ques" id="ques678"><strong>Question 679. Describe What Redo Logs Are? </strong></a></p>
<p><span class="ans"><strong>Answer :</strong></span><p>Redo logs are logical and physical structures that are designed to hold all the changes made to a database and are intended to aid in the recovery of a database.</p></p>
</li><br><br><li class="quesans mb-20">
<p><a class="accordion-trigger ques" id="ques679"><strong>Question 680. How Would You Force A Log Switch? </strong></a></p>
<p><span class="ans"><strong>Answer :</strong></span><p>ALTER SYSTEM SWITCH LOGFILE;</p></p>
</li><br><br><li class="quesans mb-20">
<p><a class="accordion-trigger ques" id="ques680"><strong>Question 681. What Does Coalescing A Tablespace Do? </strong></a></p>
<p><span class="ans"><strong>Answer :</strong></span><p>Coalescing is only valid for dictionary-managed tablespaces and de-fragments space by combining neighboring free extents into large single extents.</p></p>
</li><br><br><li class="quesans mb-20">
<p><a class="accordion-trigger ques" id="ques681"><strong>Question 682. What Is The Difference Between A Temporary Tablespace And A Permanent Tablespace? </strong></a></p>
<p><span class="ans"><strong>Answer :</strong></span><p>A temporary tablespace is used for temporary objects such as sort structures while permanent tablespaces are used to store those objects meant to be used as the true objects of the database.</p></p>
</li><br><br><li class="quesans mb-20">
<p><a class="accordion-trigger ques" id="ques682"><strong>Question 683. Name A Tablespace Automatically Created When You Create A Database?</strong></a></p>
<p><span class="ans"><strong>Answer :</strong></span><p>The SYSTEM tablespace.</p></p>
</li><br><br><li class="quesans mb-20">
<p><a class="accordion-trigger ques" id="ques683"><strong>Question 684. When Creating A User, What Permissions Must You Grant To Allow Them To Connect To The Database? </strong></a></p>
<p><span class="ans"><strong>Answer :</strong></span><p>Grant the CONNECT to the user.</p></p>
</li><br><br><li class="quesans mb-20">
<p><a class="accordion-trigger ques" id="ques684"><strong>Question 685. How Do You Add A Data File To A Tablespace ?</strong></a></p>
<p><span class="ans"><strong>Answer :</strong></span><p>ALTER TABLESPACE &lt;tablespace_name&gt; ADD DATAFILE &lt;datafile_name&gt; SIZE;</p></p>
</li><br><br><li class="quesans mb-20">
<p><a class="accordion-trigger ques" id="ques685"><strong>Question 686. How Do You Resize A Data File? </strong></a></p>
<p><span class="ans"><strong>Answer :</strong></span><p>ALTER DATABASE DATAFILE &lt;datafile_name&gt; RESIZE &lt;new_size&gt;;</p></p>
</li><br><br><li class="quesans mb-20">
<p><a class="accordion-trigger ques" id="ques686"><strong>Question 687. What View Would You Use To Look At The Size Of A Data File? </strong></a></p>
<p><span class="ans"><strong>Answer :</strong></span><p>DBA_DATA_FILES.</p></p>

</li><br><br><li class="quesans mb-20">
<p><a class="accordion-trigger ques" id="ques688"><strong>Question 689. How Would You Determine Who Has Added A Row To A Table? </strong></a></p>
<p><span class="ans"><strong>Answer :</strong></span><p>Turn on fine grain auditing for the table.</p></p>
</li><br><br><li class="quesans mb-20">
<p><a class="accordion-trigger ques" id="ques689"><strong>Question 690. How Can You Rebuild An Index? </strong></a></p>
<p><span class="ans"><strong>Answer :</strong></span><p>ALTER INDEX &lt;index_name&gt; REBUILD;</p></p>
</li><br><br><li class="quesans mb-20">
<p><a class="accordion-trigger ques" id="ques690"><strong>Question 691. Explain What Partitioning Is And What Its Benefit Is?</strong></a></p>
<p><span class="ans"><strong>Answer :</strong></span><p>Partitioning is a method of taking large tables and indexes and splitting them into smaller, more manageable pieces.</p></p>
</li><br><br><li class="quesans mb-20">
<p><a class="accordion-trigger ques" id="ques691"><strong>Question 692. You Have Just Compiled A Pl/sql Package But Got Errors, How Would You View The Errors? </strong></a></p>

<p><a class="accordion-trigger ques" id="ques692"><strong>Question 693. How Can You Gather Statistics On A Table? </strong></a></p>

</li><br><br><li class="quesans mb-20">
<p><a class="accordion-trigger ques" id="ques693"><strong>Question 694. How Can You Enable A Trace For A Session? </strong></a></p>
<p><span class="ans"><strong>Answer :</strong></span><p>Use the DBMS_SESSION.SET_SQL_TRACE; </p>
<p>or</p>
<p>Use ALTER SESSION SET SQL_TRACE = TRUE;</p></p>
</li><br><br><li class="quesans mb-20">
<p><a class="accordion-trigger ques" id="ques694"><strong>Question 695. What Is The Difference Between The Sql*loader And Import Utilities? </strong></a></p>
<p><span class="ans"><strong>Answer :</strong></span><p>These two Oracle utilities are used for loading data into the database. The difference is that the import utility relies on the data being produced by another Oracle utility EXPORT while the SQL*Loader utility allows data to be loaded that has been produced by other utilities from different data sources just so long as it conforms to ASCII formatted or delimited files.</p></p>
</li><br><br><li class="quesans mb-20">
<p><a class="accordion-trigger ques" id="ques695"><strong>Question 696. Name Two Files Used For Network Connection To A Database?</strong></a></p>
<p><span class="ans"><strong>Answer :</strong></span><p>TNSNAMES.ORA and SQLNET.ORA.</p></p>
</li><br><br><li class="quesans mb-20">
<p><a class="accordion-trigger ques" id="ques696"><strong>Question 697. What Is The Function Of Optimizer ?</strong></a></p>
<p><span class="ans"><strong>Answer :</strong></span><p>The goal of the optimizer is to choose the most efficient way to execute a SQL statement.</p></p>
</li><br><br><li class="quesans mb-20">
<p><a class="accordion-trigger ques" id="ques697"><strong>Question 698. What Is Execution Plan ? </strong></a></p>
<p><span class="ans"><strong>Answer :</strong></span><p>The combinations of the steps the optimizer chooses to execute a statement is called an execution plan.</p></p>
</li><br><br><li class="quesans mb-20">
<p><a class="accordion-trigger ques" id="ques698"><strong>Question 699. What Is Save Point ? </strong></a></p>
<p><span class="ans"><strong>Answer :</strong></span><p>For long transactions that contain many SQL statements, intermediate markers or savepoints can be declared which can be used to divide a transaction into smaller parts. This allows the option of later rolling back all work performed from the current point in the transaction to a declared savepoint within the transaction.</p></p>
</li><br><br><li class="quesans mb-20">
<p><a class="accordion-trigger ques" id="ques699"><strong>Question 700. What Are The Values That Can Be Specified For Optimizer Mode Parameter ? </strong></a></p>
<p><span class="ans"><strong>Answer :</strong></span><p>COST and RULE.</p></p>
</li><br><br><li class="quesans mb-20">
<p><a class="accordion-trigger ques" id="ques700"><strong>Question 701. Can One Rename A Tablespace? </strong></a></p>
<p><span class="ans"><strong>Answer :</strong></span><p>No, this is listed as Enhancement Request 148742.</p>
<p><em><strong>Workaround: </strong></em></p>
<ul>
<li>Export all of the objects from the tablespace</li>
<li>Drop the tablespace including contents</li>
<li>Recreate the tablespace</li>
<li>Import the objects</li>
</ul></p>
</li><br><br><li class="quesans mb-20">
<p><a class="accordion-trigger ques" id="ques701"><strong>Question 702. What Is Rule-based Approach To Optimization ? </strong></a></p>
<p><span class="ans"><strong>Answer :</strong></span><p>Choosing an executing planbased on the access paths available and the ranks of these access paths.</p></p>
</li><br><br><li class="quesans mb-20">
<p><a class="accordion-trigger ques" id="ques702"><strong>Question 703. What Are The Values That Can Be Specified For Optimizer_goal Parameter Of The Alter Session Command ?</strong></a></p>
<p><span class="ans"><strong>Answer :</strong></span><p>CHOOSE, ALL_ROWS, FIRST_ROWS and RULE.</p></p>
</li><br><br><li class="quesans mb-20">
<p><a class="accordion-trigger ques" id="ques703"><strong>Question 704. What Are The Responsibilities Of A Database Administrator ? </strong></a></p>
<p><span class="ans"><strong>Answer :</strong></span><p>Installing and upgrading the Oracle Server and application tools. Allocating system storage and planning future storage requirements for the database system. Managing primary database structures (tablespaces) Managing primary objects (table,views,indexes) Enrolling users and maintaining system security. Ensuring compliance with Oralce license agreement Controlling and monitoring user access to the database. Monitoring and optimizing the performance of the database. Planning for backup and recovery of database information. Maintain archived data on tape Backing up and restoring the database. Contacting Oracle Corporation for technical support.</p></p>
</li><br><br><li class="quesans mb-20">
<p><a class="accordion-trigger ques" id="ques704"><strong>Question 705. What Is A Trace File And How Is It Created ? </strong></a></p>
<p><span class="ans"><strong>Answer :</strong></span><p>Each server and background process can write an associated trace file. When an internal error is detected by a process or user process, it dumps information about the error to its trace. This can be used for tuning the database.</p></p>
</li><br><br><li class="quesans mb-20">
<p><a class="accordion-trigger ques" id="ques705"><strong>Question 706. What Are The Roles And User Accounts Created Automatically With The Database? </strong></a></p>
<p><span class="ans"><strong>Answer :</strong></span><p><em><strong>DBA:</strong></em> role Contains all database system privileges.</p>
<p><em><strong>SYS user account:</strong></em> The DBA role will be assigned to this account. All of the base tables and views for the database's dictionary are store in this schema and are manipulated only by ORACLE. </p>
<p><em><strong>SYSTEM user account:</strong></em> It has all the system privileges for the database and additional tables and views that display administrative information and internal tables and views used by oracle tools are created using this username.</p></p>
</li><br><br><li class="quesans mb-20">
<p><a class="accordion-trigger ques" id="ques706"><strong>Question 707. What Is The Difference Between Online And Offline Backups? </strong></a></p>
<p><span class="ans"><strong>Answer :</strong></span><p>A hot backup is a backup performed while the database is online and available for read / write. Except for Oracle exports, one can only do on-line backups when running in ARCHIVELOG mode.</p>
<p>A cold backup is a backup performed while the database is off-line and unavailable to its users.</p></p>
</li><br><br><li class="quesans mb-20">
<p><a class="accordion-trigger ques" id="ques707"><strong>Question 708. What Is The Difference Between Restoring And Recovering?</strong></a></p>
<p><span class="ans"><strong>Answer :</strong></span><p>Restoring involves copying backup files from secondary storage (backup media) to disk. This can be done to replace damaged files or to copy/move a database to a new location.  Recovery is the process of applying redo logs to the database to roll it forward. One can roll-forward until a specific point-in-time (before the disaster occurred), or roll-forward until the last transaction recorded in the log files. Sql&gt; connect SYS as SYSDBA Sql&gt; RECOVER DATABASE UNTIL TIME '2001-03-06: 16: 00: 00' USING BACKUP CONTROLFILE;</p></p>
</li><br><br><li class="quesans mb-20">
<p><a class="accordion-trigger ques" id="ques708"><strong>Question 709. How Does One Backup A Database Using The Export Utility?</strong></a></p>
<p><span class="ans"><strong>Answer :</strong></span><p>Oracle exports are "logical" database backups (not physical) as they extract data and logical definitions from the database into a file. Other backup strategies normally back-up the physical data files.</p>
<p>One of the advantages of exports is that one can selectively re-import tables, however one cannot roll-forward from an restored export file. To completely restore a database from an export file one practically needs to recreate the entire database.  Always do full system level exports (FULL=YES). Full exports include more information about the database in the export file than user level exports.</p></p>
</li><br><br><li class="quesans mb-20">
<p><a class="accordion-trigger ques" id="ques709"><strong>Question 710. What Are The Built_ins Used The Display The Lov? </strong></a></p>
<p><span class="ans"><strong>Answer :</strong></span><p>Show_lov, List_values.</p></p>
</li><br><br><li class="quesans mb-20">
<p><a class="accordion-trigger ques" id="ques710"><strong>Question 711. How Do You Call Other Oracle Products From Oracle Forms? </strong></a></p>
<p><span class="ans"><strong>Answer :</strong></span><p>Run_product is a built-in, Used to invoke one of the supported oracle tools products and specifies the name of the document or module to be run. If the called product is unavailable at the time of the call, Oracle Forms returns a message to the operator.</p></p>
</li><br><br><li class="quesans mb-20">
<p><a class="accordion-trigger ques" id="ques711"><strong>Question 712. What Is The Main Difference Between Reports 2.0 &amp; Reports 2.5? </strong></a></p>
<p><span class="ans"><strong>Answer :</strong></span><p>Report 2.5 is object oriented.</p></p>
</li><br><br><li class="quesans mb-20">
<p><a class="accordion-trigger ques" id="ques712"><strong>Question 713. What Are The Built-ins To Display The User-named Editor? </strong></a></p>
<p><span class="ans"><strong>Answer :</strong></span><p>A user named editor can be displayed programmatically with the built in procedure SHOW-EDITOR, EDIT_ TETITEM independent of any particular text item.</p></p>
</li><br><br><li class="quesans mb-20">
<p><a class="accordion-trigger ques" id="ques713"><strong>Question 714. How Many Number Of Columns A Record Group Can Have? </strong></a></p>
<p><span class="ans"><strong>Answer :</strong></span><p>A record group can have an unlimited number of columns of type CHAR, LONG, NUMBER, or DATE provided that the total number of column does not exceed 64K.</p></p>
</li><br><br><li class="quesans mb-20">
<p><a class="accordion-trigger ques" id="ques714"><strong>Question 715. What Is A Query Record Group? </strong></a></p>
<p><span class="ans"><strong>Answer :</strong></span><p>A query record group is a record group that has an associated SELECT statement. The columns in a query record group derive their default names, data types, had lengths from the database columns referenced in the SELECT statement. The records in query record group are the rows retrieved by the query associated with that record group.</p></p>
</li><br><br><li class="quesans mb-20">
<p><a class="accordion-trigger ques" id="ques715"><strong>Question 716. What Does The Term Panel Refer To With Regard To Pages? </strong></a></p>
<p><span class="ans"><strong>Answer :</strong></span><p>A panel is the number of physical pages needed to print one logical page.</p></p>
</li><br><br><li class="quesans mb-20">
<p><a class="accordion-trigger ques" id="ques716"><strong>Question 717. What Is A Master Detail Relationship? </strong></a></p>
<p><span class="ans"><strong>Answer :</strong></span><p>A master detail relationship is an association between two base table blocks- a master block and a detail block. The relationship between the blocks reflects a primary key to foreign key relationship between the tables on which the blocks are based.</p></p>
</li><br><br><li class="quesans mb-20">
<p><a class="accordion-trigger ques" id="ques717"><strong>Question 718. What Is A Library? </strong></a></p>
<p><span class="ans"><strong>Answer :</strong></span><p>A library is a collection of subprograms including user named procedures, functions and packages.</p></p>
</li><br><br><li class="quesans mb-20">
<p><a class="accordion-trigger ques" id="ques718"><strong>Question 719. What Is An Anchoring Object &amp; What Is Its Use? What Are The Various Sub Events A Mouse Double Click Event Involves? </strong></a></p>
<p><span class="ans"><strong>Answer :</strong></span><p>An anchoring object is a print condition object which used to explicitly or implicitly anchor other objects to itself.</p></p>
</li><br><br><li class="quesans mb-20">
<p><a class="accordion-trigger ques" id="ques719"><strong>Question 720. Use The Add_group_column Function To Add A Column To Record Group That Was Created At A Design Time? </strong></a></p>
<p><span class="ans"><strong>Answer :</strong></span><p>False.</p></p>

<p><a class="accordion-trigger ques" id="ques720"><strong>Question 721. What Is The Use Of Break Group? What Are The Various Sub Events A Mouse Double Click Event Involves?</strong></a></p>
<p><span class="ans"><strong>Answer :</strong></span><p>A break group is used to display one record for one group ones. While multiple related records in other group can be displayed.</p></p>
</li><br><br><li class="quesans mb-20">
<p><a class="accordion-trigger ques" id="ques721"><strong>Question 722. What Tuning Indicators Can One Use? </strong></a></p>
<p><span class="ans"><strong>Answer :</strong></span><p>The following high-level tuning indicators can be used to establish if a database is performing optimally or not:</p>
<ul>
<li>Buffer Cache Hit Ratio.</li>
<p><em><strong>Formula:</strong></em> Hit Ratio = (Logical Reads - Physical Reads) / Logical Reads.</p>
<p><em><strong>Action:</strong></em> Increase DB_CACHE_SIZE (DB_BLOCK_BUFFERS prior to 9i) to increase hit ratio.</p>
<li>Library Cache Hit Ratio.</li>
<p><em><strong>Action:</strong></em> Increase the SHARED_POOL_SIZE to increase hit ratio.</p>
</ul></p>
</li><br><br><li class="quesans mb-20">
<p><a class="accordion-trigger ques" id="ques722"><strong>Question 723. What Tools / Utilities Does Oracle Provide To Assist With Performance Tuning?</strong></a></p>
<p><span class="ans"><strong>Answer :</strong></span><p>Oracle provide the following tools/ utilities to assist with performance monitoring and tuning:</p>
<ul>
<li>TKProf</li>
<li>UTLBSTAT.SQL and UTLESTAT.SQL - Begin and end stats monitoring</li>
<li>Statspack</li>
<li>Oracle Enterprise Manager: Tuning Pack</li>
</ul></p>
</li><br><br><li class="quesans mb-20">
<p><a class="accordion-trigger ques" id="ques723"><strong>Question 724. What Are The Common Rman Errors (with Solutions)? </strong></a></p>
<p><span class="ans"><strong>Answer :</strong></span><p>Some of the common RMAN errors are: </p>
<p><em><strong>RMAN-20242:</strong></em> Specification does not match any archivelog in the recovery catalog.</p>
<p><em><strong>Add to RMAN script:</strong></em> sql 'alter system archive log current' .</p>
<p><em><strong>RMAN-06089:</strong></em> archived log xyz not found or out of sync with catalog.</p>
<p><em><strong>Execute from RMAN:</strong></em> change archivelog all validate;</p></p>
</li><br><br><li class="quesans mb-20">

</li><br><br><li class="quesans mb-20">
<p><a class="accordion-trigger ques" id="ques730"><strong>Question 731. What Is Hit Ratio ? </strong></a></p>
<p><span class="ans"><strong>Answer :</strong></span><p>It is a measure of well the data cache buffer is handling requests for data. Hit Ratio = (Logical Reads - Physical Reads - Hits Misses) / Logical Reads.</p></p>
</li><br><br><li class="quesans mb-20">
<p><a class="accordion-trigger ques" id="ques731"><strong>Question 732. How Do U Implement The If Statement In The Select Statement ?</strong></a></p>

<p>e.g. select DECODE (EMP_CAT,'1','First','2','Second'Null); </p>
<p>Here the Null is the else statement where null is done .</p></p>
</li><br><br><li class="quesans mb-20">

<li>User Defined Exceptions</li>

<p><a class="accordion-trigger ques" id="ques737"><strong>Question 738. How Does One Manage Oracle Database Users? </strong></a></p>
<p><span class="ans"><strong>Answer :</strong></span><p>Oracle user accounts can be locked, unlocked, forced to choose new passwords, etc. For example, all accounts except SYS and SYSTEM will be locked after creating an Oracle9iDB database using the DB Configuration Assistant (dbca). DBA's must unlock these accounts to make them available to users. </p>
<p>Look at these examples: </p>
<p>ALTER USER scott ACCOUNT LOCK -- lock a user account.<br/>
ALTER USER scott ACCOUNT UNLOCK; -- unlocks a locked users account.<br/>
ALTER USER scott PASSWORD EXPIRE; -- Force user to choose a new password.</p></p>
</li><br><br><li class="quesans mb-20">
<p><a class="accordion-trigger ques" id="ques738"><strong>Question 739. What Is The Use Of Tables Option In Exp Command ? </strong></a></p>

<p><span class="ans"><strong>Answer :</strong></span><p>Object Linking &amp; Embedding provides you with the capability to integrate objects from many Ms-Windows applications into a single compound document creating integrated applications enables you to use the features form .</p></p>

<p>e.g. DBMS_OUTPUT put_line.</p></p>

<p><a class="accordion-trigger ques" id="ques746"><strong>Question 747. What Are The Return Values Of Functions Sqlcode And Sqlerrm ? What Is Pragma Execption_init ? Explain The Usage ? </strong></a></p>
<p><span class="ans"><strong>Answer :</strong></span><p><em><strong>SQLCODE</strong></em> - returns the latest code of the error that has occurred.</p>
<p><em><strong>SQLERRM</strong></em> - returns the relevant error message of the SQLCODE.</p></p>

</li><br><br><li class="quesans mb-20">
<p><a class="accordion-trigger ques" id="ques750"><strong>Question 751. What Is Pl/sql Table ? </strong></a></p>
<p><span class="ans"><strong>Answer :</strong></span><p>Objects of type TABLE are called "PL/SQL tables", which are modeled as (but not the same as) database tables, PL/SQL tables use a primary PL/SQL tables can have one column and a primary key Cursors.</p></p>
</li><br><br><li class="quesans mb-20">
<p><a class="accordion-trigger ques" id="ques751"><strong>Question 752. What Is Rman ?</strong></a></p>
<p><span class="ans"><strong>Answer :</strong></span><p>Recovery Manager is a tool that manages the process of creating backups and also manages the process of restoring and recovering from them.</p></p>
</li><br><br><li class="quesans mb-20">
<p><a class="accordion-trigger ques" id="ques752"><strong>Question 753. Explain Union, Minus, Union All, Intersect ?</strong></a></p>
<p><span class="ans"><strong>Answer :</strong></span><p><em><strong>INTERSECT</strong></em> - returns all distinct rows selected by both queries.</p>
<p><em><strong>MINUS</strong></em> - returns all distinct rows selected by the first query but not by the second.</p>
<p><em><strong>UNION</strong></em> - returns all distinct rows selected by either query.</p>
<p><em><strong>UNION ALL</strong></em> - returns all rows selected by either query, including all duplicates.</p></p>
</li><br><br><li class="quesans mb-20">
<p><a class="accordion-trigger ques" id="ques753"><strong>Question 754. Should The Oem Console Be Displayed At All Times (when There Are Scheduled Jobs)? </strong></a></p>
<p><span class="ans"><strong>Answer :</strong></span><p>When a job is submitted the agent will confirm the status of the job. When the status shows up as scheduled, you can close down the OEM console. The processing of the job is managed by the OIA (Oracle Intelligent Agent). The OIA maintains a .jou file in the agent's subdirectory. When the console is launched communication with the Agent is established and the contents of the .jou file (binary) are reported to the console job subsystem. Note that OEM will not be able to send e-mail and paging notifications when the Console is not started.</p></p>
</li><br><br><li class="quesans mb-20">
<p><a class="accordion-trigger ques" id="ques754"><strong>Question 755. Difference Between Substr And Instr ? </strong></a></p>
<p><span class="ans"><strong>Answer :</strong></span><p>INSTR (String1,String2(n,(m)), INSTR returns the position of the mth occurrence of the string 2 instring1. The search begins from nth position of string1. SUBSTR (String1 n,m) SUBSTR returns a character string of size m in string1, starting from nth position of string1.</p></p>
</li><br><br><li class="quesans mb-20">
<p><a class="accordion-trigger ques" id="ques755"><strong>Question 756. What Kind Of Jobs Can One Schedule With Oem? </strong></a></p>
<p><span class="ans"><strong>Answer :</strong></span><p>OEM comes with pre-defined jobs like Export, Import, run OS commands, run sql scripts, SQL*Plus commands etc. It also gives you the flexibility of scheduling custom jobs written with the TCL language.</p></p>
</li><br><br><li class="quesans mb-20">
<p><a class="accordion-trigger ques" id="ques756"><strong>Question 757. What Is The Oracle Intelligent Agent? </strong></a></p>
<p><span class="ans"><strong>Answer :</strong></span><p>The Oracle Intelligent Agent (OIA) is an autonomous process that needs to run on a remote node in the network to make the node OEM manageable. The Oracle Intelligent Agent is responsible for:</p>
<ul>
<li>Discovering targets that can be managed (Database Servers, Net8 Listeners, etc.);</li>
<li>Monitoring of events registered in Enterprise Manager; and</li>
<li>Executing tasks associated with jobs submitted to Enterprise Manager.</li>
</ul></p>
</li><br><br><li class="quesans mb-20">
<p><a class="accordion-trigger ques" id="ques757"><strong>Question 758. What Is A Display Item? </strong></a></p>
<p><span class="ans"><strong>Answer :</strong></span><p>Display items are similar to text items but store only fetched or assigned values. Operators cannot navigate to a display item or edit the value it contains.</p></p>
</li><br><br><li class="quesans mb-20">

<p><a class="accordion-trigger ques" id="ques760"><strong>Question 761. What Do You Mean By A Block In Forms4.0? </strong></a></p>
<p><span class="ans"><strong>Answer :</strong></span><p>Block is a single mechanism for grouping related items into a functional unit for storing, displaying and manipulating records.</p></p>
</li><br><br><li class="quesans mb-20">
<p><a class="accordion-trigger ques" id="ques761"><strong>Question 762. How Is Possible To Restrict The User To A List Of Values While Entering Values For Parameters? </strong></a></p>

</li><br><br><li class="quesans mb-20">
<p><a class="accordion-trigger ques" id="ques762"><strong>Question 763. What Is Sql*loader And What Is It Used For? </strong></a></p>
<p><span class="ans"><strong>Answer :</strong></span><p>SQL*Loader is a bulk loader utility used for moving data from external files into the Oracle database. Its syntax is similar to that of the DB2 Load utility, but comes with more options. SQL*Loader supports various load formats, selective loading, and multi-table loads.</p></p>
</li><br><br><li class="quesans mb-20">
<p><a class="accordion-trigger ques" id="ques763"><strong>Question 764. How Can A Cross Product Be Created? </strong></a></p>
<p><span class="ans"><strong>Answer :</strong></span><p>By selecting the cross products tool and drawing a new group surrounding the base group of the cross products.</p></p>
</li><br><br><li class="quesans mb-20">
<p><a class="accordion-trigger ques" id="ques764"><strong>Question 765. What Is The Difference Between Boiler Plat Images And Image Items? </strong></a></p>
<p><span class="ans"><strong>Answer :</strong></span><p>Boiler plate Images are static images (Either vector or bit map) that you import from the file system or database to use a graphical elements in your form, such as company logos and maps. Image items are special types of interface controls that store and display either vector or bitmap images. Like other items that store values, image items can be either base table items(items that relate directly to database columns) or control items. The definition of an image item is stored as part of the form module FMB and FMX files, but no image file is actually associated with an image item until the item is populate at run time.</p></p>
</li><br><br><li class="quesans mb-20">
<p><a class="accordion-trigger ques" id="ques765"><strong>Question 766. What Are The Triggers Available In The Reports?</strong></a></p>
<p><span class="ans"><strong>Answer :</strong></span><p>Before report, Before form, After form , Between page, After report.</p></p>
</li><br><br><li class="quesans mb-20">
<p><a class="accordion-trigger ques" id="ques766"><strong>Question 767. Why Is A Where Clause Faster Than A Group Filter Or A Format Trigger? </strong></a></p>
<p><span class="ans"><strong>Answer :</strong></span><p>Because, in a where clause the condition is applied during data retrieval than after retrieving the data.</p></p>
</li><br><br><li class="quesans mb-20">
<p><a class="accordion-trigger ques" id="ques767"><strong>Question 768. What Is The Difference Between The Conventional And Direct Path Loader? </strong></a></p>
<p><span class="ans"><strong>Answer :</strong></span><p>The conventional path loader essentially loads the data by using standard INSERT statements. The direct path loader (DIRECT=TRUE) bypasses much of the logic involved with that, and loads directly into the Oracle data files. More information about the restrictions of direct path loading can be obtained from the Utilities Users Guide.</p></p>
</li><br><br><li class="quesans mb-20">

<p><a class="accordion-trigger ques" id="ques770"><strong>Question 771. What Is The Difference Between A Procedure And A Function ? </strong></a></p>
<p><span class="ans"><strong>Answer :</strong></span><p>Functions return a single variable by value whereas procedures do not return any variable by value. Rather they return multiple variables by passing variables by reference through their OUT parameter.</p></p>

</li><br><br><li class="quesans mb-20">
<p><a class="accordion-trigger ques" id="ques785"><strong>Question 786. What Are The Values Of :new And :old In Insert / Delete / Update Triggers ? </strong></a></p>
<p><span class="ans"><strong>Answer :</strong></span><p><em><strong>INSERT</strong></em> : new = new value, old = NULL.</p>
<p><em><strong>DELETE </strong></em>: new = NULL, old = old value.</p>
<p><em><strong>UPDATE </strong></em>: new = new value, old = old value.</p></p>
</li><br><br><li class="quesans mb-20">
<p><a class="accordion-trigger ques" id="ques786"><strong>Question 787. What Are Cascading Triggers? What Is The Maximum No Of Cascading Triggers At A Time? </strong></a></p>
<p><span class="ans"><strong>Answer :</strong></span><p>When a statement in a trigger body causes another trigger to be fired, the triggers are said to be cascading. Max = 32.</p></p>
</li><br><br><li class="quesans mb-20">
<p><a class="accordion-trigger ques" id="ques787"><strong>Question 788. What Are Mutating Triggers ? </strong></a></p>
<p><span class="ans"><strong>Answer :</strong></span><p>A trigger giving a SELECT on the table on which the trigger is written.</p></p>
</li><br><br><li class="quesans mb-20">
<p><a class="accordion-trigger ques" id="ques788"><strong>Question 789. What Are Constraining Triggers ? </strong></a></p>
<p><span class="ans"><strong>Answer :</strong></span><p>A trigger giving an Insert / Update on a table having referential integrity constraint on the triggering table.</p></p>
</li><br><br><li class="quesans mb-20">
<p><a class="accordion-trigger ques" id="ques789"><strong>Question 790. Describe Oracle Database's Physical And Logical Structure ? </strong></a></p>
<p><span class="ans"><strong>Answer :</strong></span><p><em><strong>Physical </strong></em>: Data files, Redo Log files, Control file.</p>
<p><em><strong>Logical </strong></em>: Tables, Views, Tablespaces, etc.</p></p>
</li><br><br><li class="quesans mb-20">

<p><a class="accordion-trigger ques" id="ques797"><strong>Question 798. Can Check Constraint Be Used For Self Referential Integrity ? How ? </strong></a></p>

</li><br><br><li class="quesans mb-20">
<p><a class="accordion-trigger ques" id="ques813"><strong>Question 814. If All The Values From A Cursor Have Been Fetched And Another Fetch Is Issued, The Output Will Be : Error, Last Record Or First Record ? </strong></a></p>
<p><span class="ans"><strong>Answer :</strong></span><p>Last Record.</p></p>
</li><br><br><li class="quesans mb-20">
<p><a class="accordion-trigger ques" id="ques814"><strong>Question 815. Is Sysdate A System Variable Or A System Function? </strong></a></p>
<p><span class="ans"><strong>Answer :</strong></span><p>System Function.</p></p>
</li><br><br><li class="quesans mb-20">
<p><a class="accordion-trigger ques" id="ques815"><strong>Question 816. Consider A Sequence Whose Currval Is 1 And Gets Incremented By 1 By Using The Nextval Reference We Get The Next Number 2. Suppose At This Point We Issue An Rollback And Again Issue A Nextval. What Will The Output Be ? </strong></a></p>
<p><span class="ans"><strong>Answer :</strong></span><p>3.</p></p>
</li><br><br><li class="quesans mb-20">
<p><a class="accordion-trigger ques" id="ques816"><strong>Question 817. Definition Of Relational Database By Dr. Codd (ibm)? </strong></a></p>
<p><span class="ans"><strong>Answer :</strong></span><p>A Relational Database is a database where all data visible to the user is organized strictly as tables of data values and where all database operations work on these tables.</p></p>
</li><br><br><li class="quesans mb-20">
<p><a class="accordion-trigger ques" id="ques817"><strong>Question 818. What Is Multi Threaded Server (mta) ? </strong></a></p>
<p><span class="ans"><strong>Answer :</strong></span><p>In a Single Threaded Architecture (or a dedicated server configuration) the database manager creates a separate process for each database user. But in MTA the database manager can assign multiple users (multiple user processes) to a single dispatcher (server process), a controlling process that queues request for work thus reducing the databases memory requirement and resources.</p></p>
</li><br><br><li class="quesans mb-20">
<p><a class="accordion-trigger ques" id="ques818"><strong>Question 819. Which Are Initial Rdbms, Hierarchical &amp; Network Database? </strong></a></p>
<p><span class="ans"><strong>Answer :</strong></span><p><em><strong>RDBMS </strong></em>- R system.</p>
<p><em><strong>Hierarchical </strong></em>- IMS.</p>
<p><em><strong>Network </strong></em>- DBTG.</p></p>
</li><br><br><li class="quesans mb-20">
<p><a class="accordion-trigger ques" id="ques819"><strong>Question 820. What Is Functional Dependency?</strong></a></p>
<p><span class="ans"><strong>Answer :</strong></span><p>Given a relation R, attribute Y of R is functionally dependent on attribute X of R if and only if each X - value has associated with it precisely one -Y value in R.</p></p>
</li><br><br><li class="quesans mb-20">
<p><a class="accordion-trigger ques" id="ques820"><strong>Question 821. While Designing In Client/server What Are The 2 Important Things To Be Considered ? </strong></a></p>
<p><span class="ans"><strong>Answer :</strong></span><p>Network Overhead (traffic), Speed and Load of client server.</p></p>
</li><br><br><li class="quesans mb-20">
<p><a class="accordion-trigger ques" id="ques821"><strong>Question 822. When To Create Indexes ? </strong></a></p>
<p><span class="ans"><strong>Answer :</strong></span><p>To be created when table is queried for less than 2% or 4% to 25% of the table rows.</p></p>
</li><br><br><li class="quesans mb-20">
<p><a class="accordion-trigger ques" id="ques822"><strong>Question 823. How Can You Avoid Indexes ? </strong></a></p>
<p><span class="ans"><strong>Answer :</strong></span><p>TO make index access path unavailable - Use FULL hint to optimizer for full table scan - Use INDEX or AND - EQUAL hint to optimizer to use one index or set to indexes instead of another. - Use an expression in the Where Clause of the SQL..</p></p>
</li><br><br><li class="quesans mb-20">

<p><a class="accordion-trigger ques" id="ques830"><strong>Question 831. What Is The Difference Between Foreign Key And Reference Key ? </strong></a></p>

</li><br><br><li class="quesans mb-20">
<p><a class="accordion-trigger ques" id="ques834"><strong>Question 835. What Is A Forward Declaration ? What Is Its Use ? </strong></a></p>
<p><span class="ans"><strong>Answer :</strong></span><p>PL/SQL requires that you declare an identifier before using it. Therefore, you must declare a subprogram before calling it. This declaration at the start of a subprogram is called forward declaration. A forward declaration consists of a subprogram specification terminated by a semicolon.</p></p>
</li><br><br><li class="quesans mb-20">
<p><a class="accordion-trigger ques" id="ques835"><strong>Question 836. What Are Actual And Formal Parameters ? </strong></a></p>
<p><span class="ans"><strong>Answer :</strong></span><p><em><strong>Actual Parameters</strong></em> : Subprograms pass information using parameters. The variables or expressions referenced in the parameter list of a subprogram call are actual parameters. For example, the following procedure call lists two actual parameters named emp_num and amount:</p>
<p>Eg. raise_salary(emp_num, amount);</p>
<p><em><strong>Formal Parameters </strong></em>: The variables declared in a subprogram specification and referenced in the subprogram body are formal parameters. For example, the following procedure declares two formal parameters named emp_id and increase:</p>
<p>Eg. PROCEDURE raise_salary (emp_id INTEGER, increase REAL) IS current_salary REAL;</p></p>
</li><br><br><li class="quesans mb-20">
<p><a class="accordion-trigger ques" id="ques836"><strong>Question 837. What Are The Types Of Notation ? </strong></a></p>
<p><span class="ans"><strong>Answer :</strong></span><p>Position, Named, Mixed and Restrictions.</p></p>
</li><br><br><li class="quesans mb-20">
<p><a class="accordion-trigger ques" id="ques837"><strong>Question 838. What Are Various Types Of Joins ? </strong></a></p>
<p><span class="ans"><strong>Answer :</strong></span><p>Equijoins, Non-equijoins, self join, outer join.</p></p>
</li><br><br><li class="quesans mb-20">
<p><a class="accordion-trigger ques" id="ques838"><strong>Question 839. What Is A Package Cursor ? </strong></a></p>
<p><span class="ans"><strong>Answer :</strong></span><p>A package cursor is a cursor which you declare in the package specification without an SQL statement. The SQL statement for the cursor is attached dynamically at runtime from calling procedures.</p></p>
</li><br><br><li class="quesans mb-20">
<p><a class="accordion-trigger ques" id="ques839"><strong>Question 840. If You Insert A Row In A Table, Then Create Another Table And Then Say Rollback. In This Case Will The Row Be Inserted ? </strong></a></p>
<p><span class="ans"><strong>Answer :</strong></span><p>Yes. Because Create table is a DDL which commits automatically as soon as it is executed. The DDL commits the transaction even if the create statement fails internally (eg table already exists error) and not syntactically.</p></p>
</li><br><br><li class="quesans mb-20">
<p><a class="accordion-trigger ques" id="ques840"><strong>Question 841. What Are The Various Types Of Queries ?</strong></a></p>

<li>Normal Queries</li>
<li>Sub Queries</li>
<li>Co-related queries</li>
<li>Nested queries</li>
<li>Compound queries.</li>
</ul></p>
</li><br><br><li class="quesans mb-20">
<p><a class="accordion-trigger ques" id="ques841"><strong>Question 842. What Is Implicit Cursor And How Is It Used By Oracle ? </strong></a></p>
<p><span class="ans"><strong>Answer :</strong></span><p>An implicit cursor is a cursor which is internally created by Oracle. It is created by Oracle for each individual SQL.</p></p>
</li><br><br><li class="quesans mb-20">

</li><br><br><li class="quesans mb-20">
<p><a class="accordion-trigger ques" id="ques843"><strong>Question 844. What Is Pl/sql? </strong></a></p>
<p><span class="ans"><strong>Answer :</strong></span><p>PL/SQL is Oracle's Procedural Language extension to SQL. The language includes object oriented programming techniques such as encapsulation, function overloading, information hiding (all but inheritance), and so, brings state-of-the-art programming to the Oracle database server and a variety of Oracle tools.</p></p>
</li><br><br><li class="quesans mb-20">
<p><a class="accordion-trigger ques" id="ques844"><strong>Question 845. Is There A Pl/sql Engine In Sql*plus? </strong></a></p>
<p><span class="ans"><strong>Answer :</strong></span><p>No. Unlike Oracle Forms, SQL*Plus does not have a PL/SQL engine. Thus, all your PL/SQL are send directly to the database engine for execution. This makes it much more efficient as SQL statements are not stripped off and send to the database individually.</p></p>
</li><br><br><li class="quesans mb-20">

To avoid the cost of licensing you may suggest the clients may decide to permanently close their older GL Periods, such that historical records can be archived.</p></p>

</li><br><br><li class="quesans mb-20">
<p><a class="accordion-trigger ques" id="ques854"><strong>Question 855. What Is The Significance Of Profile Option "node Trust Level" In Oracle Apps?</strong></a></p>
<p><span class="ans"><strong>Answer :</strong></span><p>If this profile option is set to a value of external against a server, then it signifies that the specific mid-tier is External i.e. it will be exposed to the www. In other words this server is not within the firewall of your client. The idea behind this profile option is to flag such middle-tier so that special restrictions can be applied against its security, which means a very restricted set of responsibilities will be available from such Middle-Tier.</p></p>
</li><br><br><li class="quesans mb-20">
<p><a class="accordion-trigger ques" id="ques855"><strong>Question 856. What Is The Significance Of Profile Option "responsibility Trust Level"?</strong></a></p>
<p><span class="ans"><strong>Answer :</strong></span><p>In order to make a responsibility accessible from an external web tier, you must set profile option “Responsibility Trust Level” at responsibility level to “External”. Only those responsibilities that have this profile option against them will be accessible from External Middle tiers.</p></p>
</li><br><br><li class="quesans mb-20">
<p><a class="accordion-trigger ques" id="ques856"><strong>Question 857. What Else Can You Suggest To Restrict The Access To Screens From External Web Tiers?</strong></a></p>

<p><a class="accordion-trigger ques" id="ques857"><strong>Question 858. What Is The Role Of Document Manager In Oracle Purchasing?</strong></a></p>
<p><span class="ans"><strong>Answer :</strong></span><p>POXCON is an immediate concurrent program. It receives pipe signal from the application when a request is made for approval / reservations / receipts.</p></p>

<p><a class="accordion-trigger ques" id="ques864"><strong>Question 865. What Is The Difference Between Running Gather Stats And "program - Optimizer [rgoptm]" In Oracle General Ledger?</strong></a></p>
<p><span class="ans"><strong>Answer :</strong></span><p>“Gather Stats” will simply gather the stats against existing tables, indexes etc. However Gather Stats does not create any new indexes. But “Program – Optimizer[RGOPTM]” can create indexes on GL_CODE_COMBINATIONS, provided accounting segment has the indexed flag enabled.</p></p>
</li><br><br><li class="quesans mb-20">
<p><a class="accordion-trigger ques" id="ques865"><strong>Question 866. You Have Written A Piece Of Code In Por_custom_pkg For Oracle Iprocurement, But Its Not Taking Any Effect? What May Be The Reason?</strong></a></p>
<p><span class="ans"><strong>Answer :</strong></span><p>Depending upon which procedure in POR_ CUSTOM_ PKG has been programmed, one or more of the below profile options must be set to Yes.</p>
<p><em><strong>POR</strong></em>: Enable Req Header Customization<br/>
<em><strong>POR</strong></em>: Enable Requisition Line Customization<br/>
<em><strong>POR</strong></em>: Enable Req Distribution Customization.</p></p>
</li><br><br><li class="quesans mb-20">
<p><a class="accordion-trigger ques" id="ques866"><strong>Question 867. What Is The Key Benefit Of Punching Out To Suppliers Catalogs Rather Than Loading Their Catalogs Locally In Oracle Iprocurement?</strong></a></p>
<p><span class="ans"><strong>Answer :</strong></span><p>Punchout has several advantages like, Catalogs don’t need to be loaded locally saves space on your system. You can get up-to-date list of catalogs by punching out and also you get the benefit of up-to-date pricing information on vendor items.</p></p>

<p><a class="accordion-trigger ques" id="ques868"><strong>Question 869. Does Oracle Grants Use Its Own Schema Or Does It Uses Oracle Project Accounting Schema?</strong></a></p>
<p><span class="ans"><strong>Answer :</strong></span><p>Although Oracle Grants has its own schema i.e. GMS, it reuses many of the tables with in Oracle Projects Schema like PA_ PROJECTS_ ALL, PA_ EXPENDITURE_ ITEMS_ ALL, PA_ EXPENDITURE_ TYPES etc.</p></p>

<p><a class="accordion-trigger ques" id="ques869"><strong>Question 870. What Are The Settings Needed For Printing Bitmap Reports?</strong></a></p>

</li><br><br><li class="quesans mb-20">
<p><a class="accordion-trigger ques" id="ques870"><strong>Question 871. For A Pl/sql Based Concurrent Program Do You Have To Issue A Commit At The End?</strong></a></p>
<p><span class="ans"><strong>Answer :</strong></span><p>The concurrent program runs within its own new session. In APPS, the default database setting enforces a commit at the end of each session. Hence no explicit COMMIT is required.</p></p>
</li><br><br><li class="quesans mb-20">
<p><a class="accordion-trigger ques" id="ques871"><strong>Question 872. What Is The Best  Way To Add Debugging To The Code In Apps?</strong></a></p>
<p><span class="ans"><strong>Answer :</strong></span><p>Use fnd_log.string , i.e. FND Logging. Behind the scenes Oracles FND Logging uses autonomous transaction to insert records in a table named fnd_log_messages.</p>
<p>For example</p>
<pre>
DECLARE
BEGIN
fnd_log.STRING(log_level =&gt; fnd_log.level_statement
   ,module=&gt;'xxxx '||'pkg/procedurename '
   ,message=&gt;'your debug message here');
END ;
</pre>
<div>Three profile options effecting FND Logging are</div>
<div> </div>
<div>FND: Debug Log Mode.<br/>
FND: Debug Log Enabled.<br/>
FND: Debug Log Module.</div>
<p> </p></p>
</li><br><br><li class="quesans mb-20">
<p><a class="accordion-trigger ques" id="ques872"><strong>Question 873. If You Wish To Trigger Of An Update Or Insert In Bespoke Table Or Take Some Action In Response To A Tca Record Being Created Or Modified, How Would You Do It? Will You Write A Database Triggers On Tca Tables?</strong></a></p>
<p><span class="ans"><strong>Answer :</strong></span><p>There are various pre-defined Events that are invoked from the Oracle TCA API’s.</p>
<p>TCA was Oracle’s first initiative towards a fully API based approach, which means the screen and the processes all use the same set of APIs for doing same task. In order to take an action when these events occur, you can subscribe a custom PL/SQL procedure or a Custom Workflow to these events. Some of the important TCA events are listed below:-</p>
<p>oracle.apps.ar.hz.ContactPoint.update<br/>
oracle.apps.ar.hz.CustAccount.create<br/>
oracle.apps.ar.hz.CustAccount.update<br/>
oracle.apps.ar.hz.CustAcctSite.create<br/>
oracle.apps.ar.hz.CustAcctSite.update<br/>
oracle.apps.ar.hz.CustAcctSiteUse.create<br/>

<p><a class="accordion-trigger ques" id="ques878"><strong>Question 879. How Would You Know If The Purchase Order Xml Has Been Transmitted To Vendor, Looking At The Tables?</strong></a></p>
<p><span class="ans"><strong>Answer :</strong></span><p>The  XML delivery status can be found from a table named ecx_oxta_logmsg. Use the  query below</p>
<pre>
SELECT edoc.document_number,
decode(eol.result_code, 1000,'Success','Failure')AS status,
eol. result_ text
FROM  ecx_oxta_ logmsg eol,
ecx_ doclogs edoc, ecx_ outbound_ logs eog
WHERE edoc. msgid = eol. sender_ message_ id
AND eog. out_ msgid = edoc. msgid
ORDER  BY edoc. document_ number</pre></p>
